class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-166-672976" title="Sasha Chavkin, ‘Xinjiang’s architect of mass detention: Zhu Hailun’, ICIJ, 24 November 2019."><sup>&nbsp;[166]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>并早在2010年就提出了一个名为“大政法委”的治理模式。</p><p>朱海仑于2006年至2009年期间担任新疆政法委书记。<span id="easy-footnote-167-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-167-672976" title="‘Resume of Comrade Zhu Hailun’ [朱海仑同志简历], People’s Daily Online [人民网], November 2011."><sup>&nbsp;[167]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>2009年乌鲁木齐七五事件后，朱接替了被免职的栗智，成为新任乌鲁木齐市委书记。为了恢复秩序，朱提出了“大政法委”的概念，<span id="easy-footnote-168-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-168-672976" title=" 王鼎, ‘Great transformation led to great development’ [大变革促大发展], Xinjiang Daily [新疆日报], 23 November 2014."><sup>&nbsp;[168]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>以求革新维稳工作，具体方法包括加强情报搜集、提高各警卫机构间的协调，以及基层动员。<span id="easy-footnote-169-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-169-672976" title=" 杨晓钗, ‘Zhu Hailun: the pioneer who leads the capital of the western region’ [朱海仑: 西域首府引路人], China Youth News [中华儿女新闻网], 19 September 2012."><sup>&nbsp;[169]&nbsp;</sup></a></span></p><p>更重要的是，“大政法委”也标志着乌鲁木齐对网格化管理和“三位一体”机制的早期实践。2010年，“大政法委”在乌鲁木齐的四个中心区搞试点，其中就包括阿布力孜一家居住的水磨沟区。试点一年后，乌市新增了16900个监控摄像头、16个居委会和八个派出所，每个居委会的开支和工作人员是原来的三倍多。<span id="easy-footnote-170-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-170-672976" title="Zhou Ju [周桔], Li Jing [李静], ‘Problems and countermeasures in Ürümqi neighbourhood grid-style management’ [乌鲁木齐城市社区网格化管理存在的问题与对策], Journal of the Ürümqi Municipal Party School [中共乌鲁木齐市委党校学报], March 2012; Zhu Hailun [朱海仑], ‘Improve the environment and push for leaps and bounds in urban science’ [优化环境 推动城市科学跨越], CCP Members Net [共产党员网], 11 September 2012; Yang Xiaochai, ‘Zhu Hailun: the pioneer who leads the capital of the western region’, China Youth Net, 19 September 2019."><sup>&nbsp;[170]&nbsp;</sup></a></span></p><p>在陈全国上任后，朱海仑于2016年11月复任新疆政法委书记。第二年，他签署了《关于进一步加强和规范职业技能教育培训中心工作的意见》，该文件后来被泄露给“国际调查记者联盟”。<span id="easy-footnote-171-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-171-672976" title="‘Official telegram: Opinions regarding further reinforcement and standardisation of the work of vocational education and training centres’ [自治区机关发电: 关于进一步加强和规范职业技能教育培训中心工作的意见], Xinjiang PLAC via ICIJ, online; Chavkin, ‘Xinjiang’s architect of mass detention: Zhu Hailun’."><sup>&nbsp;[171]&nbsp;</sup></a></span></p><h2>第五章：把法律变成武器</h2><p>在政法委的领导下，新疆的政法系统推动了两场运动中最具压迫性的政策，包括法外拘留体系和正式的监禁制度。据估计，这两种制度分别拘留了数十万人，而且往往未经过正当程序。<span id="easy-footnote-172-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-172-672976" title="Gene A Bunin, ‘The elephant in the XUAR: II. Brand new prisons, expanding old prisons, and hundreds of thousands of new inmates’, Art of Life in Chinese Central Asia, 4 January 2021."><sup>&nbsp;[172]&nbsp;</sup></a></span></p><p>与过去的“运动式执法”类似，<span id="easy-footnote-173-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-173-672976" title="Lang Peijuan, ‘Characteristics and disadvantages of “fire-fighting” style governance’, People’s Daily Magazine, 15 July 2016."><sup>&nbsp;[173]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>在新疆的运动中，执法决定往往仓促、严厉又任意。为了满足运动的需要，高级官员颁布了与现存法律法规相抵触的新规。在基层，官员则公开夸耀不按法律规定行事，并获得高级官员和国家媒体的支持。各级官员被要求向党宣誓效忠，保持“政治坚定”。</p><div class="ar-caption">图14：2017年，新疆监狱系统的官员集体宣誓对党忠诚。</div><div id="attachment_672728" style="width: 616px" class="wp-caption aligncenter"><noscript><img aria-describedby="caption-attachment-672728" src="https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/xj-5.png" alt="" width="606" height="202" class="size-full wp-image-672728" srcset="https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/xj-5.png 606w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/xj-5-300x100.png 300w" sizes="(max-width: 606px) 100vw, 606px"></noscript><img aria-describedby="caption-attachment-672728" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns=%22http://www.w3.org/2000/svg%22%20viewBox=%220%200%20606%20202%22%3E%3C/svg%3E" data-src="https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/xj-5.png" alt="" width="606" height="202" class="lazyload size-full wp-image-672728" data-srcset="https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/xj-5.png 606w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/xj-5-300x100.png 300w" data-sizes="(max-width: 606px) 100vw, 606px"><p id="caption-attachment-672728" class="wp-caption-text">来源：新疆监狱系统广大党员干部集体发声亮剑 / 新疆监狱管理局 2017年6月10日（<a href="https://archive.ph/wip/7ORMv">链接</a>）</p></div><p>2014年，在反恐运动开始几天后，新疆高级警官马飞写道：</p><p>“对辖区最不放心的极端宗教分子一定要想尽一切办法把他们送到最放心的地方去——看守所，请别给我谈什么犯罪的构成要件，要件成立了，人头就落地了。打击极端宗教宁可过激不可放纵……”<span id="easy-footnote-174-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-174-672976" title="The author first published this piece on his own WeChat account in 2014. ‘The sentiments of a front-line public security bureau chief in southern Xinjiang’ [一个南疆一线公安局长的感悟], ‘Military Pomegranate Seeds’ on WeChat [微信公众号”武装的石榴籽”], 2 June 2014. "><sup>&nbsp;[174]&nbsp;</sup></a></span></p><p>马飞的话后来被国家媒体和一家知名的智库报道。<span id="easy-footnote-175-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-175-672976" title="Southern Xinjiang frontline public security bureau chief: To solve frequent violent terrorism (we) should rely on “offense”’ [南疆一线公安局长：解决暴恐多发要靠’进攻’], Sina News [新浪网], 4 August 2014."><sup>&nbsp;[175]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>, <span id="easy-footnote-176-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-176-672976" title="Ma Feng, ‘The sentiments of a front-line public security chief in southern Xinjiang’ [马飞: 一个南疆一线公安局长的感悟!], Kunlunce Research Institute on WeChat [昆仑策研究院微信公众号], 16 July 2017."><sup>&nbsp;[176]&nbsp;</sup></a></span></p><p>同年，新疆自治区高级人民法院宣布将把审判工作与揭批工作相结合，开始召开公判大会。<span id="easy-footnote-177-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-177-672976" title="‘Xinjiang High People’s Court’, State Council Information Office, 23 December 2014, online; ‘Pang Congwu, ‘Xinjiang High People’s Court’, Legal Daily, 23 December 2014. "><sup>&nbsp;[177]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>如本报告第二章所述，公判大会是一种政治表演，在当代中国已被取缔并受到广泛批评。</p><p>2014年5月，新疆北部城市伊宁市举行了一场引人瞩目的公判大会。被指控为“分裂分子”和“恐怖分子”的人被一车一车拉到体育场，其中大部分是维吾尔人，他们的头被警察按着，在7000人的注视下被判刑。<span id="easy-footnote-178-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-178-672976" title="Li Xin’an [李新安], ‘Xinjiang’s Ili Prefecture conducts mass public sentencing, public arrest and public detention and publicly sentencing 55 defendants’ [新疆伊犁州举行公判、公捕、公拘大会 对55名被告人公开宣判], People’s Daily Online [人民网], 27 May 2014."><sup>&nbsp;[178]&nbsp;</sup></a></span></p><div class="ar-caption">图15：伊宁市在体育场举行公判大会有7000人参加，现场有武装军人安保。</div><div id="attachment_672729" style="width: 614px" class="wp-caption aligncenter"><noscript><img aria-describedby="caption-attachment-672729" src="https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/xj-6.png" alt="" width="604" height="200" class="size-full wp-image-672729" srcset="https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/xj-6.png 604w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/xj-6-300x99.png 300w" sizes="(max-width: 604px) 100vw, 604px"></noscript><img aria-describedby="caption-attachment-672729" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns=%22http://www.w3.org/2000/svg%22%20viewBox=%220%200%20604%20200%22%3E%3C/svg%3E" data-src="https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/xj-6.png" alt="" width="604" height="200" class="lazyload size-full wp-image-672729" data-srcset="https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/xj-6.png 604w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/xj-6-300x99.png 300w" data-sizes="(max-width: 604px) 100vw, 604px"><p id="caption-attachment-672729" class="wp-caption-text">来源：新疆伊犁州举行公判、公捕、公拘大会 对55名被告人公开宣判 / 人民网 2014年5月27日（<a href="https://web.archive.org/web/20200502003931/http://politics.people.com.cn/n/2014/0527/c1001-25072595.html">链接</a>）</p></div><p>时任伊宁市政法委书记黎明辉在现场表示要“以雷霆之势坚决把敌人的嚣张气焰打下去，绝对取得反恐维稳严打这场人民战争的最终胜利。”<span id="easy-footnote-179-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-179-672976" title="Ibid. "><sup>&nbsp;[179]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>第二年，黎明辉的上级领导、时任新疆政法委书记熊选国指示新疆高级人民法院“继续加大公开审判力度，到案发地去，把公开宣判与公开揭批有机结合起来，扩大审判效果，有力震慑暴恐犯罪分子，确保新疆社会大局稳定”。<span id="easy-footnote-180-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-180-672976" title="Wang Shulin [王书林], ‘Always place top priority on strike hard during trials’ [始终把严打置于审判工作的重中之重], People’s Court Daily [人民法院报], 8 June 2015."><sup>&nbsp;[180]&nbsp;</sup></a></span></p><p>2016年，阿勒泰市公安局在社交媒体上发表声明，称反恐运动就意味着“从严从重顶格处罚”。</p><p>“新疆目前处于严打暴恐时期。严打就意味着从严从重顶格处罚，本来可以判缓刑的就判实刑；按照刑法可以判处3年或10年的，肯定判你10年。”<span id="easy-footnote-181-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-181-672976" title="‘Never repost or disseminate violent terrorist audio or videos! Otherwise, the consequences will be very serious!’ [切勿转发传播暴力恐怖音视频! 否则后果很严重!], Altay City Public Security [阿勒泰市公安], 13 March 2016."><sup>&nbsp;[181]&nbsp;</sup></a></span></p><p>2014年，新疆高院还明确下令加快审判速度<span id="easy-footnote-182-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-182-672976" title="‘Xinjiang High People’s Court demands’, State Council Information Office, 23 December 2014, online; Pang Congwu, ‘Xinjiang High People’s Court’, Legal Daily, 23 December 2014."><sup>&nbsp;[182]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>——这种策略类似于1983年的严打运动，当时约有170万人在4年时间内被判刑。<span id="easy-footnote-183-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-183-672976" title="Lang Peijuan, ‘Characteristics and disadvantages of “fire-fighting” style governance’, China University of Political Science and Law, 15 July 2016."><sup>&nbsp;[183]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>在严打期间，司法机关抛开正常的刑事程序，用所谓“联合办案”来达到前所未有的审判速度，导致了大量不公正、虚假和错误的判决出台，包括死刑判决。<span id="easy-footnote-184-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-184-672976" title="Ibid. "><sup>&nbsp;[184]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>在新疆，被拘留者的命运也由所谓的“政法联席会议”来决定。<span id="easy-footnote-185-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-185-672976" title="‘Ürümqi Public Security Bureau, Shuimogou District Branch, Xinxing Street Police Station, Xinmin West Street Neighbourhood Police Substation’ (乌鲁木齐市公安局水磨沟区分局新兴街派出所新民西街社区警务室), Ürümqi Police Records, 28 February 2018."><sup>&nbsp;[185]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>与新疆的镇压类似，1983年严打运动在六个月的时间里导致56.3万人被判处劳动改造和再教育。<span id="easy-footnote-187-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-187-672976" title="Tanner, Strike hard! Anti-crime campaigns and Chinese criminal justice, 1979–1985, p. 98.<br /><span id='easy-footnote-186-672976' class='easy-footnote-margin-adjust'></span><span class='easy-footnote'><a href='#easy-footnote-bottom-186-672976' title=''><sup>&amp;nbsp;[186]&amp;nbsp;</sup></a></span>Ramzy &amp;amp; Buckley, ‘“Absolutely no mercy”: Leaked files expose how China organized mass detentions of Muslims’"><sup>&nbsp;[187]&nbsp;</sup></a></span></p><p>2017年，新疆书记陈全国多次指示官员做到“应收尽收”。<span id="easy-footnote-188-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-188-672976" title="The New York Times, 16 November 2019 ."><sup>&nbsp;[188]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>同年，朱海仑作为政法委书记命令地、县级党委书记亲自监督再教育工作。<span id="easy-footnote-189-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-189-672976" title="‘Official telegram’, Xinjiang PLAC via ICIJ, 2017."><sup>&nbsp;[189]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>然而，直到2018年10月9日新疆才修订了《新疆去极端化条例》以允许地方政府设立“职业技能教育培训中心”及其他“教育转化机构”。至此，新疆的大批拘留和思想灌输设施才有了迟来的法律根据。<span id="easy-footnote-190-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-190-672976" title="Liu Caiyu, Liu Xuanzun, ‘Xinjiang revises its anti-extremism regulation’, Global Times, 10 October 2018, online; ‘New revision to “Xinjiang De-Extremification Regulation” published’ [新修订版《新疆维吾尔自治区去极端化条例》发布], Standing Committee of Xinjiang People’s Congress [新疆自治区人大常委会] via National Security and Anti-Terrorism Information Net [国家安全-反恐怖主义信息网], 9 October 2018."><sup>&nbsp;[190]&nbsp;</sup></a></span></p><p>在这两次运动中，新疆官员的其他违法行为不胜枚举，包括判决书和记录的缺失，法律文件的编造，以及将维吾尔人和其他原住民群体的宗教和文化行为定为犯罪。<span id="easy-footnote-191-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-191-672976" title="Gene A Bunin, ‘The elephant in the XUAR: III. “In accordance with the law”’, Art of Life in Central Asia, 19 April 2021."><sup>&nbsp;[191]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>正如研究人员斌吉恩（Gene Bunin）指出，哪怕是在中国国内的背景下，新疆当局的执法方式也是“完全不合理并且严重违法的”。<span id="easy-footnote-192-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-192-672976" title="Ibid."><sup>&nbsp;[192]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>举例说明：</p><p>2017年9月14日，乌鲁木齐市SY-150号便民警务站的日志写道，拆迁项目在即，居委会干部曾试图强迫被拘留者的亲属搬离天山区明华街：</p><p>“你们家中有人被公安机关收押审查，你们不能再（在）这儿购房居住，如果你们不及时搬走，将你们全家收押。”<span id="easy-footnote-193-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-193-672976" title="‘Ürümqi Public Security Bureau, convenience police station SY-150’ (便民警务室SY-150), Ürümqi Police Records, 14 September 2017."><sup>&nbsp;[193]&nbsp;</sup></a></span></p><div class="ar-caption">图16：再教育运动开始时，昌吉州的官员在乌鲁木齐考察GX-001号便民警务站。</div><div id="attachment_672730" style="width: 614px" class="wp-caption aligncenter"><noscript><img aria-describedby="caption-attachment-672730" src="https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/xj-7.png" alt="" width="604" height="385" class="size-full wp-image-672730" srcset="https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/xj-7.png 604w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/xj-7-300x191.png 300w" sizes="(max-width: 604px) 100vw, 604px"></noscript><img aria-describedby="caption-attachment-672730" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns=%22http://www.w3.org/2000/svg%22%20viewBox=%220%200%20604%20385%22%3E%3C/svg%3E" data-src="https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/xj-7.png" alt="" width="604" height="385" class="lazyload size-full wp-image-672730" data-srcset="https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/xj-7.png 604w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/xj-7-300x191.png 300w" data-sizes="(max-width: 604px) 100vw, 604px"><p id="caption-attachment-672730" class="wp-caption-text">来源：昌吉州代表团来乌鲁木齐市考察交流维稳工作 / 新浪新闻 2017年6月2日（<a href="https://archive.ph/XmzpW">链接</a>）</p></div><p>2019年，一名新疆官员对“人权观察”表示，在再教育运动的一个时期里：</p><p>“每个地区都下了抓人指标，于是我们开始到处乱抓：跟邻居吵架的，街头打架的，酗酒的，游手好闲的；我们把这些人抓来，指控他们搞极端主义。中心的空间收不了这么多人，他们就盖新的……”<span id="easy-footnote-194-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-194-672976" title="‘China: Big data program targets Xinjiang’s Muslims’, Human Rights Watch, 9 December 2020."><sup>&nbsp;[194]&nbsp;</sup></a></span></p><p>乌鲁木齐警方文件也揭示出基层官员的类似的行为。一份警方报告称，2017年，维吾尔男子伊克热木·伊明被拘留，后来在达坂城拘留所接受再教育，他在那里感染了乙肝和梅毒。<span id="easy-footnote-195-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-195-672976" title="‘Ürümqi Public Security Bureau, Shuimogou District Branch, Shuimogou Police Station’ [乌鲁木齐市公安局水磨沟区分局水磨沟派出所], Ürümqi Police Records, 15 January 2019, online; ‘Profile of Ekrem Imin’, Xinjiang Victims Database"><sup>&nbsp;[195]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>拘留所不仅没有为他治疗乙肝，而且不允许他的妻子给他送药。伊明被告知，他被拘留只是因为“社区民警凑数字”。<span id="easy-footnote-196-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-196-672976" title="Ibid. "><sup>&nbsp;[196]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>据估计，达板城拘留所能够同时关押一万人，是新疆、也是中国最大的拘留所。<span id="easy-footnote-197-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-197-672976" title="Dake Kang, ‘Room for 10,000: Inside China’s largest detention center’, The Associated Press, 22 July 2021, online. "><sup>&nbsp;[197]&nbsp;</sup></a></span></p><p>2017年10月3日，维吾尔妇女古孜力阿依·买买提司拉木被幸福路派出所拘留。她被认为是“对社会不满的不放心人员”，因此被送入再教育营。<span id="easy-footnote-198-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-198-672976" title="‘Ürümqi Public Security Bureau, Shuimogou District Public Branch, Shuimogou Police Station, Wenxi Neighbourhood Police Substation’ [乌鲁木齐市公安局水磨沟区分局水磨沟派出所温西社区警务室], Ürümqi Police Records, 29 November 2018"><sup>&nbsp;[198]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>艾可帕尔·吐尔逊的情况相似。警察记录写道：“自2014年与妻子离婚后，一直在外地做生意，电话也多次更改，无法联系，2018年3月8日回到乌市，经社区园桌会议研判，因此人居无定所，无固定收入，不易管控，2018年3月10日教育转化。”<span id="easy-footnote-199-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-199-672976" title="‘Ürümqi Public Security Bureau, Shuimogou District Branch, Shuimogou Police Station’ [乌鲁木齐市公安局水磨沟区分局水磨沟派出所], Ürümqi Police Records, 18 March 2019. "><sup>&nbsp;[199]&nbsp;</sup></a></span></p><div class="ar-caption">图17：阿勒泰地区检察院官员举行发声亮剑活动，手拿横幅：“对党绝对忠诚”</div><div id="attachment_672731" style="width: 606px" class="wp-caption aligncenter"><noscript><img aria-describedby="caption-attachment-672731" src="https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/xj-8.png" alt="" width="596" height="220" class="size-full wp-image-672731" srcset="https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/xj-8.png 596w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/xj-8-300x111.png 300w" sizes="(max-width: 596px) 100vw, 596px"></noscript><img aria-describedby="caption-attachment-672731" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns=%22http://www.w3.org/2000/svg%22%20viewBox=%220%200%20596%20220%22%3E%3C/svg%3E" data-src="https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/xj-8.png" alt="" width="596" height="220" class="lazyload size-full wp-image-672731" data-srcset="https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/xj-8.png 596w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/xj-8-300x111.png 300w" data-sizes="(max-width: 596px) 100vw, 596px"><p id="caption-attachment-672731" class="wp-caption-text">来源：坚定理想信念 对党绝对忠诚 做新时代忠诚干净担当的人民检察官 / 微博@新疆检察 2019年2月22日（<a href="https://archive.ph/nhcYp">链接</a>）</p></div><p>新疆“严重违法”的执法行为是习近平领导下的中国施行严刑峻法和法律工具主义的一个极端例证。通过法律改革，中国共产党在不断巩固集权，并根据自己的利益重塑司法机构。中国法律专家卡尔・明兹纳（Carl Minzner）认为，通过这一过程，中国远离了程序问责和司法独立的概念，<span id="easy-footnote-200-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-200-672976" title="Which were in theory acknowledged and embraced by Xi’s recent predecessors to some extent. Qian Gang [钱钢], ‘Who will terminate “judicial independence”?’ [谁要给“司法独立”判死刑?], FT Chinese, 19 January 2015 "><sup>&nbsp;[200]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>公开“与法律对立”。<span id="easy-footnote-201-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-201-672976" title="Carl Minzner, ‘Legal reform in the Xi Jinping era’, Asia Policy, July 2015, 20:4–6. "><sup>&nbsp;[201]&nbsp;</sup></a></span></p><p>讽刺的是，在这种转变发生的同时，官方舆论把“依法治国”称为中共治国的基石，“依法治国”也被认为是“习近平思想”的一个关键方面。<span id="easy-footnote-202-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-202-672976" title="Jacques deLisle, ‘The rule of law with Xi-era characteristics: law for economic reform, anticorruption, and illiberal politics, Asia Policy, July 2015, 20:23–29. "><sup>&nbsp;[202]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>新疆党委成立了“依法治疆委员会”，由陈全国担任主任。<span id="easy-footnote-203-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-203-672976" title="‘At the Xinjiang Party Committee conference on ruling Xinjiang in accordance with law, Chen Quanguo emphasises the need to deeply implement Xi Jinping Thought and comprehensively push the “Govern Xinjiang in accordance with law” policy to new heights’ [陈全国在自治区党委全面依法治疆委员会会议上强调：深入贯彻落实习近平法治思想，推动全面依法治疆迈上新台阶], Tianshan News [天山网], 24 May 2021"><sup>&nbsp;[203]&nbsp;</sup></a></span></p><p>“依法治国”一词曾经和社会正义与公平联系在一起，<span id="easy-footnote-204-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-204-672976" title="‘Hu Jintao chairs the the first collective study of the 17th Central Politburo’ [胡锦涛主持十七届中央政治局第一次集体学习], People’s Daily Online [人民网], 27 August 2013. "><sup>&nbsp;[204]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>并在1999年被写入中国宪法。<span id="easy-footnote-205-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-205-672976" title="Xiao Hui [肖辉], Zhang Qiao [张乔], ‘Governing the nation in accordance with law doctrine enshrined in the constitution in 1999’ [1999年依法治国写入宪法], Phoenix News [凤凰新闻], 16 September 2009. "><sup>&nbsp;[205]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>在习近平的领导下，这个词现在指的是马列主义层面上的法律，即法律是党的意志的体现；并遵循中国古老的法家思想，认为严刑峻法是实现善治的必要条件。<span id="easy-footnote-206-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-206-672976" title="Li Lin [李林], ‘The origin of Xi Jinping’s rule by law theory’, [习近平法治思想的理论渊源], Guangming Daily [光明日报] via Xinhua Net [新华网], 22 January 2021. "><sup>&nbsp;[206]&nbsp;</sup></a></span></p><p>“决不能照搬别国模式和做法，决不能走西方‘宪政’、‘三权鼎立’、‘司法独立’的路子，”习近平在一次2018年的讲话中说。<span id="easy-footnote-207-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-207-672976" title="‘Xi Jinping’s latest quotes on rule by law help to analyse the reasons why high-profile cadres commit crimes’ [习近平谈法治最新金句，剖析高级干部走上犯罪道路原因], People’s Daily Online [人民网], 15 February 2019"><sup>&nbsp;[207]&nbsp;</sup></a></span></p><h2>第六章：一线总指挥</h2><p>据中国国家媒体报道，习近平有“县委书记情结”；<span id="easy-footnote-208-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-208-672976" title="  Zhu Shuyan [朱书缘], ‘Xi Jinping’s “county party secretary complex” and how that relates to the concept of “frontline commander”’ [习近平的‘县委书记’情结：为何关注‘一线总指挥’？], People’s Daily Online [人民网], 7 June 2015, online; ‘Xi Jinping’s “county party secretary” complex: how the concept of “sesame official” relates to the rise and fall of nations’ [习近平的‘县委书记’情结：‘芝麻官’关系国家兴衰安危], People’s Daily Online [人民网], 13 January 2015, online.<br />"><sup>&nbsp;[208]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>也就是说，他对中国大约3000个县级行政部门党的一把手格外挂心。在他的治理理念中，县级党委是党的“一线指挥部”，而县委书记是“一线总指挥”，他们对党的忠诚度和动员群众的能力对党国政权的繁荣和生存至关重要。<span id="easy-footnote-209-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-209-672976" title=" Zhu Shuyan, ‘Xi Jinping’s “county party secretary complex” and how that relates to the concept of “frontline commander”.<br />"><sup>&nbsp;[209]&nbsp;</sup></a></span></p><p>在2014年至2017年期间，中央党校和中央组织部（类似于党的人事部门）为全国各地所有县委书记在北京安排了为期两个月的住校培训。<span id="easy-footnote-210-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-210-672976" title=" ‘The CCP’s “all-member training” of county party secretaries tie the “knot” of stable governance’ [中共‘全员轮训’县委书记打牢执政‘纽结’], Xinhua Net [新华网], 15 January 2015, online; Zhu Shuyan, ‘Xi Jinping’s “county party secretary complex”’, People’s Daily Online [人民网], 7 June 2015, online; Gu Baiwen [顾百文], ‘Brief discussion on joining the Central Party School county party secretary training program’ [浅谈参加中央党校县委书记研修班学习收获], Suihua Daily [绥化日报], 21 January 2015, online.<br />"><sup>&nbsp;[210]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>习近平亲自讲授了一部分课程，<span id="easy-footnote-211-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-211-672976" title="‘200 county party secretaries went to Beijing to ‘go to school’: They watch historical documentaries about the collapse of the Soviet Union in the evening’ [200县委书记进京“上学记”：晚上看苏东剧变等历史剧], Beijing News [新京报] via Xinhua Net [新华网], 16 January 2015, online.<br />"><sup>&nbsp;[211]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>并在2015年出版了一本书，为县委书记制定标准，<span id="easy-footnote-212-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-212-672976" title=" ‘“Follow the examples of Jiao Yulu as county party secretary”, written by Xi Jinping, is published’’ [习近平《做焦裕禄式的县委书记》出版发行], People’s Daily Online [人民网], 27 August 2015, online.<br />"><sup>&nbsp;[212]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>要求他们对党绝对忠诚，“做政治的明白人”。<span id="easy-footnote-213-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-213-672976" title="Xi Jinping [习近平], ‘Speech delivered upon meeting the nation’s outstanding county party secretaries’ [在会见全国优秀县委书记时的讲话], People’s Daily Online [人民网], 31 August 2015, online.<br />"><sup>&nbsp;[213]&nbsp;</sup></a></span></p><p>新疆把“一线总指挥”的说法落到了实处。县委书记直接负责许多“一把手工程”，包括在其辖区内策划反恐运动，<span id="easy-footnote-214-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-214-672976" title=" ‘Chen Quanguo emphasises stability maintenance in Xinjiang during teleconference’ [陈全国在自治区维护稳定工作电视电话上强调], Xinjiang Daily [新疆日报], 9 January 2017, online.<br />"><sup>&nbsp;[214]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>领导一个工作小组来监督职业技能教育培训服务管理局（又称教培局），<span id="easy-footnote-215-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-215-672976" title="The full name is ‘Vocational Education and Training Service Management Bureau’.  "><sup>&nbsp;[215]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>签署强迫转移劳动力的“目标责任状”，<span id="easy-footnote-216-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-216-672976" title="219   ‘Hotan Prefecture creates innovative mechanism to facilitate labour transfers’ [和田地区创新机制助推劳动力转移就业], Xinjiang Economic News [新疆经济报] via Xinhua Net [新华网], 23 May 2017, online; Yang Tingting [杨婷婷], Shi Kaiwei [石凯伟], ‘Around 1200 surplus labourers from urban and rural Lop County have traveled to other parts of China for work’ [洛浦县1200余名城乡富余劳动力赴内地务工], China Xinjiang [中国新疆], 11 May 2017, online.  "><sup>&nbsp;[216]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>以及监督人口控制政策的实施。<span id="easy-footnote-217-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-217-672976" title="‘Notice on Cherchen County’s 2018 targeted crackdown against illegal births’ [关于印发《且末县2018年度违法生育专项治理工作实施方案》的通知], Cherchen County People’s Government [且末县人民政府], 30 May 2018, online.<br />"><sup>&nbsp;[217]&nbsp;</sup></a></span></p><p>ASPI的研究人员整理了新疆数百名县委正副书记的姓名和基本信息，时间范围为2014年至2021年8月。<span id="easy-footnote-218-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-218-672976" title="Officials whose profiles are publicly available and can be corroborated by credible sources. The lists of official names are withheld from publication due to privacy concerns, but may be available upon request.<br />"><sup>&nbsp;[218]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>分析发现，在过去7年里，新疆基层“一线指挥官”绝大多数是汉人（图18）。在大多数县里，维吾尔或其他少数民族官员担任没有实权的二把手——党委副书记兼县长。尽管法律上，新疆是维吾尔自治区，但当前（2021年9月）ASPI的研究人员无法找到任何一位维吾尔族的县委书记。</p><div class="ar-caption">图18：从2013年到2021年，新疆县委书记的民族成分（上）和县委副书记兼县长的民族成分（下）</div><p><noscript><img src="https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635860952473.png" alt="file"></noscript><img class="lazyload" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns=%22http://www.w3.org/2000/svg%22%20viewBox=%220%200%20210%20140%22%3E%3C/svg%3E" data-src="https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635860952473.png" alt="file"></p><div id="attachment_672770" style="width: 510px" class="wp-caption aligncenter"><noscript><img aria-describedby="caption-attachment-672770" src="https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635860969120.png" alt="" width="500" class="size-full wp-image-672770" srcset="https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635860969120.png 984w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635860969120-300x190.png 300w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635860969120-768x487.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 984px) 100vw, 984px"></noscript><img aria-describedby="caption-attachment-672770" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns=%22http://www.w3.org/2000/svg%22%20viewBox=%220%200%20500%20333.33333333333%22%3E%3C/svg%3E" data-src="https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635860969120.png" alt="" width="500" class="lazyload size-full wp-image-672770" data-srcset="https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635860969120.png 984w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635860969120-300x190.png 300w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635860969120-768x487.png 768w" data-sizes="(max-width: 984px) 100vw, 984px"><p id="caption-attachment-672770" class="wp-caption-text">来源：ASPI</p></div><p>这些数据展示了中共对维吾尔人和其他少数民族官员体制性的不信任，以及汉人主导的党国体制内深层的种族歧视。中共最初写入中国宪法的民族自治<span id="easy-footnote-219-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-219-672976" title="  ‘Constitution of China’ [中华人民共和国宪法], Central People’s Government [中国中央人民政府], online. "><sup>&nbsp;[219]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>不复存在，只剩一批处在依附状态、用来装点门面的维吾尔官员还顶着这样的承诺自欺欺人。</p><p>在过去七年里所有的新疆县委书记当中，有三个人最受媒体和中组部称道，有时甚至受到习近平本人的表扬。为了点出新疆地方政治的动态，本章介绍这三位官员，尤其强调他们在推行两场运动的过程中发挥的作用。<span id="easy-footnote-220-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-220-672976" title=" Because the profiles are written from publicly available sources instead of interviews, they reflect only these individuals’ public personas. "><sup>&nbsp;[220]&nbsp;</sup></a></span></p><h4>“不忘初心”</h4><p>2021年7月1日是中共建党100周年。6月29日，习近平在北京人民大会堂内会见了来自全国各地的103名“优秀县委书记”。<span id="easy-footnote-221-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-221-672976" title="228  ‘Xi Jinping met with the nation’s outstanding county party secretaries’ [习近平会见全国优秀县委书记], Xinhua Net [新华网], 29 June 2021, online.  "><sup>&nbsp;[221]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>其中最年轻是一位36岁的汉人官员，名叫药宁。<span id="easy-footnote-222-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-222-672976" title="‘36 year-old Yao Ning was awarded the title of ‘The nation’s most outstanding county party secretary’, receiving congratulations from two faculties at Tsinghua University, his alma mater’ [36岁药宁获‘全国优秀县委书记’称号后，母校清华两院系祝贺], New Beijing News [新京报], 2 July 2021, online.  "><sup>&nbsp;[222]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>他因为不同寻常的教育背景而吸引了媒体的关注。与许多从地方大学或党校获得学历的干部不同，药宁在两所全世界顶尖的学府学习过——清华大学和哈佛大学。<span id="easy-footnote-223-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-223-672976" title=" ‘Alumnus of the engineering department, Yao Ning, recognised as “The nation’s outstanding county party secretary”’ [工业工程系校友药宁被授予‘全国优秀县委书记’称号], Tsinghua University Department of Industrial Engineering [清华大学工业工程系], 1 July 2021, online; ‘Ning Yao: Asia Fellow, AY 2010-2011’, Harvard Kennedy School Ash Centre for Democratic Governance and Innovation, online. "><sup>&nbsp;[223]&nbsp;</sup></a></span></p><div class="ar-caption">图19：药宁，在哈佛大学受过教育的新疆县委书记。</div><div id="attachment_672771" style="width: 510px" class="wp-caption aligncenter"><noscript><img aria-describedby="caption-attachment-672771" src="https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635861131913.png" alt="" width="500" class="size-full wp-image-672771" srcset="https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635861131913.png 1198w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635861131913-300x199.png 300w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635861131913-1024x679.png 1024w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635861131913-768x509.png 768w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635861131913-1080x716.png 1080w" sizes="(max-width: 1198px) 100vw, 1198px"></noscript><img aria-describedby="caption-attachment-672771" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns=%22http://www.w3.org/2000/svg%22%20viewBox=%220%200%20500%20333.33333333333%22%3E%3C/svg%3E" data-src="https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635861131913.png" alt="" width="500" class="lazyload size-full wp-image-672771" data-srcset="https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635861131913.png 1198w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635861131913-300x199.png 300w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635861131913-1024x679.png 1024w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635861131913-768x509.png 768w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635861131913-1080x716.png 1080w" data-sizes="(max-width: 1198px) 100vw, 1198px"><p id="caption-attachment-672771" class="wp-caption-text">来源：清华毕业的85后县委书记，拟获全国表彰 / 京报网 2021年5月7日（<a href="https://archive.fo/OvAkq">链接</a>）</p></div><p>2019年初，药宁被任命为巴楚县委书记。<span id="easy-footnote-224-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-224-672976" title="‘36 year-old Yao Ning was awarded the title of ‘The nation’s outstanding county party secretary’, receiving congratulations from two Schools at Tsinghua University, his Alma Mater’ [36岁药宁获‘全国优秀县委书记’称号后，母校清华两院系祝贺], New Beijing News [新京报], 2 July 2021, online.  "><sup>&nbsp;[224]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>ASPI研究人员发现，从2017年起，当局在这个以维吾尔人为主的小县城<span id="easy-footnote-225-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-225-672976" title=" Ilham Tohti [伊力哈木·土赫提], ‘Demographics of Maralbeshi County, Xinjiang’ [维吾尔自治区巴楚县民族人口结构], Uyghur Online [维吾尔在线], 25 April 2013, online; ‘Ferocious birth-control policies in Xinjiang are racially targeted’, The Economist, 26 June 2021, online.  "><sup>&nbsp;[225]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>新建或扩建了九座拘留设施。<span id="easy-footnote-226-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-226-672976" title=" Nathan Ruser, Xinjiang detention facilities dataset, ASPI, 24 September 2020, online. "><sup>&nbsp;[226]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>就在药宁到任前几个月，巴楚县当局计划招募320名再教育营工作人员；这些职位只对18岁到45岁的汉人男性开放。<span id="easy-footnote-227-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-227-672976" title=" The 2018 Xinjiang Maralbeshi County recruitment of 320 staff for vocational education and training centres’ [2018年新疆巴楚县招聘职业技能教育培训中心工作人员320名简章], Xinjiang Public Sector Net [新疆公务员网], 15 March 2018, online. "><sup>&nbsp;[227]&nbsp;</sup></a></span></p><p>作为党委书记，药宁的职责理论上包括担任巴楚县再教育营运作的总负责人，<span id="easy-footnote-228-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-228-672976" title=" See section 7.2: ‘Re-education camps’, which references Xinjiang government order that county party secretaries personally lead a taskforce that in turn oversees the operations for the detention facilities. "><sup>&nbsp;[228]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>他还应当负责大规模劳动力转移，这种转移导致维吾尔工人遭受强迫劳动和流离失所。<span id="easy-footnote-229-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-229-672976" title="See section 7.4: ‘Coercive labour assignments’, which discusses how local party and government leaders typically head the area’s labour transfer taskforce, and the coercive nature of Xinjiang’s labour transfer programs.  "><sup>&nbsp;[229]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>在最近的一次采访中，药宁公开表达了他为促进巴楚县劳动力转移政策付出的努力，<span id="easy-footnote-230-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-230-672976" title="‘Yao Ning, the nation’s outstanding county party secretary: Take root in the frontier, keep the original inspiration, shoulder the mission and fulfil the promise’ [全国优秀县委书记药宁：扎根边疆守初心，勇担使命践诺言], Xinhua All Media [新华全媒+], online.  "><sup>&nbsp;[230]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>声称在他两年任职期间，有37700人被分配了工作。<span id="easy-footnote-231-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-231-672976" title="Ibid.  "><sup>&nbsp;[231]&nbsp;</sup></a></span></p><div class="ar-caption">图20：巴楚县的一座监狱。这座监狱在药宁在职期间运转。2017年，监狱大大扩建；2021年，监狱仍有两处正在建设中。从卫星图片中可以看到，监狱有六座暸望塔。</div><div id="attachment_672772" style="width: 510px" class="wp-caption aligncenter"><noscript><img aria-describedby="caption-attachment-672772" src="https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635861227107.png" alt="" width="500" class="size-full wp-image-672772" srcset="https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635861227107.png 1196w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635861227107-300x288.png 300w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635861227107-1024x985.png 1024w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635861227107-768x738.png 768w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635861227107-1080x1038.png 1080w" sizes="(max-width: 1196px) 100vw, 1196px"></noscript><img aria-describedby="caption-attachment-672772" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns=%22http://www.w3.org/2000/svg%22%20viewBox=%220%200%20500%20333.33333333333%22%3E%3C/svg%3E" data-src="https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635861227107.png" alt="" width="500" class="lazyload size-full wp-image-672772" data-srcset="https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635861227107.png 1196w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635861227107-300x288.png 300w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635861227107-1024x985.png 1024w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635861227107-768x738.png 768w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635861227107-1080x1038.png 1080w" data-sizes="(max-width: 1196px) 100vw, 1196px"><p id="caption-attachment-672772" class="wp-caption-text">来源：ASPI<br></p></div><p>药宁正是习近平理想中的干部：年轻、忠诚、有能力。<span id="easy-footnote-232-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-232-672976" title=" 228   ‘Young cadres look here! Xi Jinping is paying attention to you!’ [年轻干部看过来! 习近平在关注你们], Xinhua Net [新华网], 3 July 2018, online. "><sup>&nbsp;[232]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>药宁在山西省长大并在清华大学学习工程学。在读书期间，他积极参与学生政治，担任班级共青团支书和年级党支部委员，并当选为学生会主席。<span id="easy-footnote-233-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-233-672976" title=" ‘Alumnus of the engineering department, Yao Ning’, Tsinghua University Department of Industrial Engineering, 1 July 2021, online. "><sup>&nbsp;[233]&nbsp;</sup></a></span></p><p>在2008年的学生会选举中，药宁就表现出非凡的爱国主义精神和政治抱负，表示希望能“奉献边疆”，“要到祖国最需要的地方去，上大舞台、做大事业”。<span id="easy-footnote-234-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-234-672976" title=" Zhang Rui [张睿], ‘Yao Ning: Go where the motherland needs me most’ [药宁: 到祖国最需要的地方去], Tsinghua University News [清华大学新闻], 25 April 2018, online. "><sup>&nbsp;[234]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>同年，药宁被清华评选为“本科生优秀党员”。<span id="easy-footnote-235-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-235-672976" title=" ‘Alumnus of the engineering department, Yao Ning’, Tsinghua University Department of Industrial Engineering, 1 July 2021, online. "><sup>&nbsp;[235]&nbsp;</sup></a></span></p><p>2010年到2011年期间，药宁在哈佛大学阿什民主治理与创新中心担任访问学者，这是他在清华大学攻读公共政策博士项目的一部分。<span id="easy-footnote-236-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-236-672976" title=" ‘Ning Yao: Asia Fellow, AY 2010–2011’, Harvard Kennedy School Ash Centre for Democratic Governance and Innovation, online.  "><sup>&nbsp;[236]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>2014年，药宁博士毕业后开始在新疆喀什地区工作，先后在维吾尔人为主的疏勒县，后来在巴楚县。</p><p>在2018年的一次清华校友访谈中，药宁为有机会在新疆为国家服务感到感激。校报记者引用他说：“在边疆工作，无论是反恐维稳还是脱贫攻坚，这份工作体验在内地其他任何地方都不可能有。”他还表示，自己的“革命浪漫主义精神”源自于母校清华大学的教育。<span id="easy-footnote-237-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-237-672976" title=" Zhang Rui, ‘Yao Ning: Go where the motherland needs him most’. "><sup>&nbsp;[237]&nbsp;</sup></a></span></p><p>有时候药宁也会提到工作中的艰难。2019年12月，他微在博上发布消息说，认识的一位新疆官员突然去世，“是被工作累死的”。</p><blockquote><p>“前几天还打电话开玩笑，一下子人就没了，心里很不是滋味，南疆能有今天的安定局面，是有多少干部为之付出啊，R.I.P.……” <span id="easy-footnote-238-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-238-672976" title="‘Yao Ning’s Weibo posts’ [药宁的微博], Weibo [微博], 25 February to 17 June 2021, online.  "><sup>&nbsp;[238]&nbsp;</sup></a></span></p></blockquote><div class="ar-caption">图21：药宁的微博</div><div id="attachment_672773" style="width: 510px" class="wp-caption aligncenter"><noscript><img aria-describedby="caption-attachment-672773" src="https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635861344836.png" alt="" width="500" class="size-full wp-image-672773" srcset="https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635861344836.png 1188w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635861344836-300x143.png 300w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635861344836-1024x488.png 1024w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635861344836-768x366.png 768w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635861344836-1080x515.png 1080w" sizes="(max-width: 1188px) 100vw, 1188px"></noscript><img aria-describedby="caption-attachment-672773" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns=%22http://www.w3.org/2000/svg%22%20viewBox=%220%200%20500%20333.33333333333%22%3E%3C/svg%3E" data-src="https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635861344836.png" alt="" width="500" class="lazyload size-full wp-image-672773" data-srcset="https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635861344836.png 1188w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635861344836-300x143.png 300w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635861344836-1024x488.png 1024w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635861344836-768x366.png 768w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635861344836-1080x515.png 1080w" data-sizes="(max-width: 1188px) 100vw, 1188px"><p id="caption-attachment-672773" class="wp-caption-text">来源：药宁的微博 / 微博 2021年2月25日到6月17日（<a href="https://archive.ph/JjO7B">链接</a>）</p></div><p>药宁的妻子周凌休同样毕业于清华大学，是来自内蒙古的蒙古人。<span id="easy-footnote-239-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-239-672976" title="The Inner Mongolia Autonomous Region. "><sup>&nbsp;[239]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>内蒙古也是中国的边疆地区，当地的语言和文化正受到党国的打压。<span id="easy-footnote-240-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-240-672976" title="Alice Su, ‘Threats of arrest, job loss and surveillance. China targets its “model minority”’, The Los Angeles Times, 23 September 2020, online; Chris Atwood, ‘Bilingual education in Inner Mongolia: an explainer’, Made in China, 30 August 2020, online.  "><sup>&nbsp;[240]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>据周凌休说，药宁在新疆承受着巨大的压力：“有几次半夜他从喀什给我打电话，平日里坚强的他竟痛哭流涕。”<span id="easy-footnote-241-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-241-672976" title="‘To go to the border town’ [去一趟边城], Tsinghua University Department of Industrial Engineering [清华大学工业工程系], 27 April 2017, online.  "><sup>&nbsp;[241]&nbsp;</sup></a></span></p><p>根据社会学教授周雪光的研究，运动式治理往往迫使官僚放弃独立处理信息、作出正确判断的能力。<span id="easy-footnote-242-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-242-672976" title="Zhou Xueguang, The institutional logic of governance in China, 2017, p. 131, online.  "><sup>&nbsp;[242]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>药宁也承认在新疆接收到的信息存在矛盾之处。在2018年的一次采访中，药宁说：“我们在边疆，每天会遇到各式各样的信息，有时这些信息还是互相矛盾的，如何去伪存真都是一件比较有难度的事情。” 他说：能够从大量的信息中做出独立的判断，对一件事情有自己独到的理解和认识是一种重要的能力。<span id="easy-footnote-243-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-243-672976" title="Zhang Rui, ‘Yao Ning: Go where the country needs him most’.  "><sup>&nbsp;[243]&nbsp;</sup></a></span></p><p>2019年初，药宁在微博上发了一张照片，里面是“为人民服务”的匾额，并配以文字：“每到特别累的时候，就把当年拍的这张照片拿出来看看，惟愿，不忘初心。”<span id="easy-footnote-244-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-244-672976" title="‘Yao Ning’s Weibo posts’ [药宁的微博], Weibo [微博], 25 February to 17 June 2021, online.  "><sup>&nbsp;[244]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>“不忘初心”是一句习近平名言，常被用来鼓励像药宁这样的基层官员为人民服务，帮助中华民族复兴。<span id="easy-footnote-245-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-245-672976" title="‘Xi focus-quotable quotes: Xi Jinping on original aspiration of Chinese Communists’, Xinhua Net English, 29 June 2020, online.  "><sup>&nbsp;[245]&nbsp;</sup></a></span></p><div class="ar-caption">图22：2021年，药宁（中）带领巴楚县干部对党旗宣誓。</div><div id="attachment_672774" style="width: 510px" class="wp-caption aligncenter"><noscript><img aria-describedby="caption-attachment-672774" src="https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635861437547.png" alt="" width="500" class="size-full wp-image-672774" srcset="https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635861437547.png 1182w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635861437547-300x199.png 300w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635861437547-1024x679.png 1024w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635861437547-768x509.png 768w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635861437547-1080x716.png 1080w" sizes="(max-width: 1182px) 100vw, 1182px"></noscript><img aria-describedby="caption-attachment-672774" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns=%22http://www.w3.org/2000/svg%22%20viewBox=%220%200%20500%20333.33333333333%22%3E%3C/svg%3E" data-src="https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635861437547.png" alt="" width="500" class="lazyload size-full wp-image-672774" data-srcset="https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635861437547.png 1182w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635861437547-300x199.png 300w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635861437547-1024x679.png 1024w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635861437547-768x509.png 768w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635861437547-1080x716.png 1080w" data-sizes="(max-width: 1182px) 100vw, 1182px"><p id="caption-attachment-672774" class="wp-caption-text">来源：巴楚县开展新党员代表入党宣誓活动，药宁领誓 / 巴楚县人民政府 2021年6月27日（<a href="https://archive.fo/AtFit">链接</a>）</p></div><h4>“拜城经验”</h4><p>在新疆的两次运动中，自治区二把手一直是党委副书记雪克来提·扎克尔，他是维吾尔人，直到2021年9月30日一直兼任新疆自治区主席。在扎克尔任内，他手下有11位副主席，其中6人是汉族，3人维吾尔族，2人其他民族。<span id="easy-footnote-246-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-246-672976" title=" As of September 2021, out of 11 vice-governors in Xinjiang, six are Han, three are Uyghur and two are from other ethnic groups. See ‘Regional leadership database &amp;#8211; Xinjiang’ [地方领导资料库:新疆], People’s Daily Online [人民网], online.  / ‘Regional leadership database: Xinjiang’ [地方领导资料库:新疆], People’s Daily Online [人民网], online. "><sup>&nbsp;[246]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>11位副主席中级别最高、权力最大的是艾尔肯·吐尼亚孜，他曾在2012年作为“新世界访问学者”在哈佛大学阿什中心访问学习过四个月。<span id="easy-footnote-247-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-247-672976" title=" ‘Resume of Erken Tuniyaz, vice-chairman and standing committee member of the Xinjiang Party Committee’ [艾尔 肯·吐尼亚孜-简历, 新疆维吾尔自治区党委常委、副主席], People’s Daily Online [人民网], online; Kate Hoagland, ‘Ash Center: Two senior Chinese officials perform key research at the Ash Center’, Harvard Kennedy School Ash Center for Democratic Governance and Innovation, 3 February 2012, online. "><sup>&nbsp;[247]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>吐尼亚孜目前代理自治区主席一职。<span id="easy-footnote-248-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-248-672976" title="  ‘Erken Tuniyaz is acting chairman of Xinjiang’ [艾尔肯·吐尼亚孜任新疆维吾尔自治区代主席], People’s Daily Online [人民网], 2 October 2021, online.<br />"><sup>&nbsp;[248]&nbsp;</sup></a></span></p><p>最近刚被提拔至副主席之列，在11位中级别最低的是50岁的汉人官员杨发森。<span id="easy-footnote-249-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-249-672976" title=" ‘Regional leadership database: Xinjiang’ [地方领导资料库:新疆], People’s Daily Online [人民网], online. "><sup>&nbsp;[249]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>他曾是2015年“优秀县委书记”称号的获得者，现在是新疆最年轻的省部级领导。<span id="easy-footnote-250-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-250-672976" title="‘“Post-70s” Yang Fasen assumes his new post and becomes the youngest provincial and ministerial level official in Xinjiang. He was once awarded the title of “outstanding county party secretary’ [70后”杨发森履新, 成新疆最年轻省部级，曾获‘全国优秀县委书记’荣誉], Sina Finance News [新浪财经新闻], 31 March 2021, online. "><sup>&nbsp;[250]&nbsp;</sup></a></span></p><p>在2009年七五到2014年反恐运动开始这段时间内，杨发森担任阿克苏地区拜城县委书记。拜城地处偏远，居民以维吾尔人为主。杨发森在那里创造了一套工作方式，后来被称为“拜城经验”。</p><div class="ar-caption">图23：2015年，杨发森在人民大会堂给习近平汇报工作。</div><div id="attachment_672775" style="width: 510px" class="wp-caption aligncenter"><noscript><img aria-describedby="caption-attachment-672775" src="https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635861575550.png" alt="" width="500" class="size-full wp-image-672775" srcset="https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635861575550.png 1192w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635861575550-300x219.png 300w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635861575550-1024x747.png 1024w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635861575550-768x561.png 768w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635861575550-1080x788.png 1080w" sizes="(max-width: 1192px) 100vw, 1192px"></noscript><img aria-describedby="caption-attachment-672775" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns=%22http://www.w3.org/2000/svg%22%20viewBox=%220%200%20500%20333.33333333333%22%3E%3C/svg%3E" data-src="https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635861575550.png" alt="" width="500" class="lazyload size-full wp-image-672775" data-srcset="https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635861575550.png 1192w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635861575550-300x219.png 300w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635861575550-1024x747.png 1024w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635861575550-768x561.png 768w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635861575550-1080x788.png 1080w" data-sizes="(max-width: 1192px) 100vw, 1192px"><p id="caption-attachment-672775" class="wp-caption-text">来源：“70后”杨发森履新, 成新疆最年轻省部级, 曾获“全国优秀县委书记”荣誉 / 新浪财经新闻 2021年3月31日（<a href="https://archive.ph/CVCB5">链接</a>）</p></div><p>“拜城经验”是一套宣传工作政策，目的是为党的“去极端化”工作带来创新和亮点。在拜城这样的小县城，杨发森看到这意味着集中国家媒体、政府网站和对外宣传的资源，建立一个超级宣传机构——“拜城县宣传中心”。<span id="easy-footnote-251-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-251-672976" title="‘Establish joint management of large scale propaganda work’ [建立齐抓共管的大宣传工作格局], Xinjiang Daily<br />[新疆日报], 29 September 2014, online."><sup>&nbsp;[251]&nbsp;</sup></a></span></p><p>宣传中心成立于2013年1月，坐拥三层楼和600平米的空间，建造成本为200万人民币（合31万4000美元）。<span id="easy-footnote-252-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-252-672976" title="‘Establish joint management of large scale propaganda work’ [建立齐抓共管的大宣传工作格局], Xinjiang Daily<br />[新疆日报], 29 September 2014, online."><sup>&nbsp;[252]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>它负责安排媒体采访、制作内容，并将统一的信息推送到不同平台上，包括广播、电视、社交媒体和村里的广播站。中心还制作并分发“文化产品”，如宣传单、折页、戏剧、绘画和顺口溜。<span id="easy-footnote-253-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-253-672976" title="Ibid."><sup>&nbsp;[253]&nbsp;</sup></a></span></p><p>拜城县一位官员对媒体表示，宣传中心就像一个蔬菜批发市场，“宣传中心干部好比是‘菜农’，各部门宣传干事、宣传员好比‘经销商’，销售对象就是全县各族干部群众”。<span id="easy-footnote-254-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-254-672976" title="Ibid."><sup>&nbsp;[254]&nbsp;</sup></a></span></p><p>“拜城经验”的另一个特点是将普通公民变为宣传员。<span id="easy-footnote-255-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-255-672976" title="‘In-depth reporting on Xinjiang’s “Bay County Experience”, part two’ [新疆‘拜城经验’深度报道之二], Tianshan News [天山网] via Phoenix News [凤凰新闻], 30 September 2014, 2, online; Zhang Chaowen [张超文], Liu Yanghui [刘旸辉], Wu Hui [吴卉], ‘Improve and innovate cultures to achieve the goal of ‘reaching people productively and effectively’:In-depth reporting on “Bay County Experience”, part three’ [改进创新文化引领实现‘到人管用有效’拜城经验深度报道之三], Sina News [新浪新闻], 1 October 2014, online."><sup>&nbsp;[255]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>在杨发森任内，“宣讲”得到了普及，各行各业的人——党员干部、律师、宗教领袖、医生、科学家、农民、企业主、妇女和年轻人都被动员起来，通过宣讲来打击“宗教极端主义”。<span id="easy-footnote-256-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-256-672976" title="‘In-depth reporting on Xinjiang’s “Bay County Experience”, part two’ [新疆‘拜城经验’深度报道之二], Tianshan News, 30 September 2014, p. 3, online."><sup>&nbsp;[256]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>尤其值得一提的是公交车司机，他们被要求向乘客进行宣传，同时要监视乘客是否有“极端主义”迹象。<span id="easy-footnote-257-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-257-672976" title="262   Wang Tao [王涛], ‘Xinjiang transportation industry promotes “Bay County Experience” in order to further efforts in “de-extremification”’ [新疆交通运输行业推广‘拜城经验’ 深入推进‘去极端化’], Tianshan News [天山网] via Sohu News [搜狐新闻], 11 April 2015, online."><sup>&nbsp;[257]&nbsp;</sup></a></span></p><div class="ar-caption">图24：2019年，拜城县“感恩伟大祖国，歌颂幸福生活”主题宣讲。</div><div id="attachment_672776" style="width: 510px" class="wp-caption aligncenter"><noscript><img aria-describedby="caption-attachment-672776" src="https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635861677418.png" alt="" width="500" class="size-full wp-image-672776" srcset="https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635861677418.png 1186w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635861677418-300x138.png 300w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635861677418-1024x471.png 1024w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635861677418-768x354.png 768w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635861677418-1080x497.png 1080w" sizes="(max-width: 1186px) 100vw, 1186px"></noscript><img aria-describedby="caption-attachment-672776" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns=%22http://www.w3.org/2000/svg%22%20viewBox=%220%200%20500%20333.33333333333%22%3E%3C/svg%3E" data-src="https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635861677418.png" alt="" width="500" class="lazyload size-full wp-image-672776" data-srcset="https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635861677418.png 1186w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635861677418-300x138.png 300w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635861677418-1024x471.png 1024w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635861677418-768x354.png 768w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635861677418-1080x497.png 1080w" data-sizes="(max-width: 1186px) 100vw, 1186px"><p id="caption-attachment-672776" class="wp-caption-text">来源：拜城县“感恩伟大祖国，歌颂幸福生活” 主题宣讲走进大宛其、老虎台乡 / 拜城县人民政府 2019年8月11日 （<a href="https://archive.ph/ggTgq">链接</a>）</p></div><p>拜城县的经验被认为是先进而富有创意的，在反恐运动期间经常被国家媒体宣传。<span id="easy-footnote-258-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-258-672976" title="‘Establish joint management of large scale propaganda work’ [建立齐抓共管的大宣传工作格局], Xinjiang Daily [新疆日报], 29 September 2014, online; ‘Report on the “Bay County Experience”, part one: Where there is innovation, there is vitality’ [‘拜城经验’启示系列报道：哪里有创新哪里就有活力], Tianshan News [天山网], 29 September 2014, online."><sup>&nbsp;[258]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>2014年下半年，杨发森被调往库车县任职。<span id="easy-footnote-259-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-259-672976" title="A Uyghur majority county in southern Xinjiang where ASPI researchers have identified three detention facilities built or expanded after 2017. See Nathan Ruser, Xinjiang detention facilities dataset, ASPI, 24 September 2020, online."><sup>&nbsp;[259]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>他离开后，新疆各地的宣传官员纷纷前往拜城县参观宣传中心，学习拜城经验。<span id="easy-footnote-260-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-260-672976" title="‘Leaders of Aksu’s Onsu County went on inspection tour in Bay County’ [阿克苏温宿县领导赴拜城县观摩], Xinjiang People’s Government [新疆维吾尔自治区人民政府], 7 November 2014, online."><sup>&nbsp;[260]&nbsp;</sup></a></span></p><p>在一个央视采访中，来自温宿县、 柯坪县、麦盖提县和阿合奇县的官员赞扬了拜城县“去极端化”的做法，称这些措施有创意、“接地气”、令人印象深刻。2014年10月，疏附县委宣传部长阿布里米提·玉素云对媒体表示，疏附县将复制拜城的经验，最迟在年底前建成一座宣传中心。<span id="easy-footnote-261-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-261-672976" title="‘[[Xinjiang News Broadcast] Learn from the Bay County Experience and further implement ‘de-extremification’ education’ [[新疆新闻联播]学习拜城经验，深入推进‘去极端化’教育], CCTV [央视网], 4 October 2014, online. "><sup>&nbsp;[261]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>到2014年底，其他几个县也成立了类似的宣传中心。<span id="easy-footnote-262-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-262-672976" title="‘Large scale de-extremification propaganda education programs created in Konasheher County, Xinjiang’ [新疆疏附 县构建‘去极端化’宣传教育大格局], chinanews.com [中国新闻网], 9 November 2014, online; ‘Chaqiliq County took the initiative to establish a large-scale news and propaganda centre in Bayingolin Prefecture’ [巴州若羌在巴州率先成立大新闻宣传中心], Xinjiang People’s Government [新疆维吾尔自治区人民政府], 16 December 2014, online."><sup>&nbsp;[262]&nbsp;</sup></a></span></p><p>杨发森是邻省甘肃人，19岁到新疆参军。<span id="easy-footnote-263-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-263-672976" title="‘“Post-70s” Yang Fasen assumes his new post and becomes the youngest provincial and ministerial level official in Xinjiang. He was once awarded the title of “outstanding county party secretary”’, online; ‘Xinjiang Kucha County party secretary: Kucha is the forefront of Xinjiang’s anti-terrorism and stability maintenance’ [新疆库车县委书记：库车是新疆反恐维稳的前沿], State Council Information Office [国务院新闻办公室], 1 July 2015, online."><sup>&nbsp;[263]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>在军队服役三年后，他成为一名办公室秘书，并慢慢获得提拔。据官方媒体报道，杨发森工作勤奋，“没有节假日，没有昼夜之分”，在反恐运动期间与警察和其他干部一起加班到深夜。<span id="easy-footnote-264-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-264-672976" title="‘Pioneers of reforms &amp;#8211; profile of an outstanding county secretary, Yang Fasen, party secretary of Kucha County’, Xinjiang Daily, 7 July 2015, online. "><sup>&nbsp;[264]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>报道称他精力充沛，“曾以《数天数》歌曲开头为干部讲群众路线”。《数天数》一歌唱的是人生短暂。<span id="easy-footnote-265-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-265-672976" title="‘Revealed: Who are the five representatives who made speeches after shaking hands with Xi Jinping?’ [揭秘：跟习近平握手以后发言的五个代表都是谁], Sohu News [搜狐新闻], 1 July 2015, online."><sup>&nbsp;[265]&nbsp;</sup></a></span></p><p>2015年7月，在获表彰的103名“优秀县委书记”当中，仅有五人在人民大会堂讲话并与习近平握手，杨发森是其中之一，<span id="easy-footnote-266-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-266-672976" title="Ibid. "><sup>&nbsp;[266]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>这在中国是巨大的荣誉。在演讲中，杨发森称海外恐怖分子将他的照片发到网上，扬言要报复他。<span id="easy-footnote-267-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-267-672976" title="‘Kucha County party secretary: Kucha is at the forefront of Xinjiang’s anti-terrorism and stability maintenance’ [新疆库车县委书记：库车是新疆反恐维稳的前沿], State Council Information Office [国务院新闻办公室], 1 July 2015, online. "><sup>&nbsp;[267]&nbsp;</sup></a></span></p><p>在2017年开始的再教育运动中，许多维吾尔人因被贴上“80后、90后不放心人员”的标签而被拘留。<span id="easy-footnote-268-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-268-672976" title="‘Big data program targets Xinjiang’s Muslims: leaked list of over 2,000 detainees demonstrates automated repression’, Human Rights Watch, 9 December 2020, online. "><sup>&nbsp;[268]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>然而，早在2015年，来自新疆的杨发森就在给习近平作报告时说，让未受过教育的年轻维吾尔人接受劳动改造可以带来稳定：</p><blockquote><p>“针对收押人员中“80后”“90后”占80%以上、高中以下文化程度占99%的特点，我们迅速启动实施“万名青年大教育大培训、促就业保稳定”计划，免费培训3万人，使那些社会闲散青年有一技之长，有事干、有钱挣、有盼头，最大限度降低风险点。</p><p>通过不懈努力，全县宗教氛围趋于淡化，各族群众明辨是非能力明显提高，反恐维稳的正能量正在形成。”</p></blockquote><p>在获得“优秀县委书记”称号后，杨发森仕途平步青云。2016年12月，他被提升为和田地区党委副书记兼政法委书记，<span id="easy-footnote-269-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-269-672976" title="‘Resume of Yang Fasen’ [杨发森:简历], People’s Daily Online [人民网], online."><sup>&nbsp;[269]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>和田地区是新疆两场运动的前线地区之一，ASPI研究人员发现这里有52个新建或扩建的拘留所。<span id="easy-footnote-270-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-270-672976" title="The Xinjiang Data Project, ASPI, Canberra, online. "><sup>&nbsp;[270]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>2018年2月，杨发森成为和田地区党委书记；<span id="easy-footnote-271-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-271-672976" title="‘Resume of Yang Fasen’, People’s Daily Online, online. "><sup>&nbsp;[271]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>2021年3月，他成为新疆最年轻的省部级官员。<span id="easy-footnote-272-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-272-672976" title="‘“Post-70s” Yang Fasen assumes his new post and becomes the youngest provincial and ministerial level official in Xinjiang. He was once awarded the title of “outstanding county party secretary”’, online. "><sup>&nbsp;[272]&nbsp;</sup></a></span></p><h4>模范少数民族</h4><p>自2017年以来，几乎每个新疆的少数民族二把手都发表过至少一份书面承诺，保证“发声亮剑”。用色调鲜明、强硬、高度重复的语言，他们保证“感党恩、听党话、跟党走”，<span id="easy-footnote-273-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-273-672976" title="‘Protect our homes | Dorbiljin County’s deputy party secretary and county magistrate Mahesu Khan Gamshafu: Labour will bring joy today and unity will bring victory tomorrow’ [守护家园｜额敏县委副书记、县长 马合苏提汗•加木沙甫： 劳动会给今天带来欢乐，团结会给明天带来胜利], Sohu News [搜狐新闻], 11 August 2017, online. "><sup>&nbsp;[273]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>“永远牢记党的恩情”。<span id="easy-footnote-274-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-274-672976" title=" ‘Konasheher County deputy party secretary of county party committee and county magistrate Rahman Omar: Always remember the kindness of the party and resolutely eradicate the “three evil forces’’’ [疏附县委副书记、县长热合曼·吾买尔：永远牢记党的恩情坚决铲除‘三股势力’], Tianshan News [天山网], 17 August 2017, online. "><sup>&nbsp;[274]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>他们发誓要“揪出”党的敌人——“禽兽不如”的“两面人”；<span id="easy-footnote-275-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-275-672976" title="282   ‘Speak up and brandish the sword: determined to struggle against the “three evil forces”’ [发声亮剑 | 坚决同‘三股势力’ 作斗争], Sohu News [搜狐新闻], 20 May 2019, online. "><sup>&nbsp;[275]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>要“铲除”“粉碎”两面人和“三股势力”；<span id="easy-footnote-276-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-276-672976" title="Ibid. "><sup>&nbsp;[276]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>要与他们“血战到底”，进行“殊死斗争”。<span id="easy-footnote-277-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-277-672976" title="‘[Speak up and brandish the sword in Hotan]: Ereti Yunus, Keriye County’s deputy party secretary and county magistrate: Be brave and strive to be the vanguard of counterterrorism and stability maintenance’ [【亮剑和田】于田县委副书记、县长 艾热提·尤努斯：正己身勇担当，争做反恐维稳先锋], Niye Zero Distance [民丰零距离] via Sohu News [搜狐新闻], 2 October 2018, online; ‘Speak up and brandish the swords!”: We must resolutely crack down on the “three evil forces” and completely eradicate “two-faced people”’ [发声亮剑:坚决打击‘三股势力’彻底铲除‘两面人’], Xinjiang Daily [新疆日报] via Sohu News [搜狐新闻], 30 August 2018, online. "><sup>&nbsp;[277]&nbsp;</sup></a></span></p><p>一些维吾尔官员表示，维吾尔人并非突厥人后裔，而是自古以来就是中华民族的一部分。<span id="easy-footnote-278-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-278-672976" title="282   ‘Iskender Keyum: Absolute loyalty to the party, fight against the enemies until the end, and pledge to safeguard the stability, harmony and unity of Xinjiang’ [斯坎旦·克尤木：对党绝对忠诚，对敌斗争到底，誓死捍卫新疆团结稳定和谐好局面], Qumul Radio [哈密电台] via Sohu News [搜狐新闻], 19 November 2018, online; Yasin Sidik, ‘Uyghurs are not Turkic descendants’ [牙生·司地克：维吾尔族不是突厥人后裔], Ürümqi Evening News (乌鲁木齐晚报) via Aisixiang [爱思想], 30 August 2018, online. "><sup>&nbsp;[278]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>一名维吾尔官员反对使用维语，称说维语就是不爱国，就是“两面人”。<span id="easy-footnote-279-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-279-672976" title="Darren Byler, ‘The “patriotism” of not speaking Uyghur’, SupChina, 2 January 2019, online. "><sup>&nbsp;[279]&nbsp;</sup></a></span></p><div class="ar-caption">图25：维吾尔官员吾布力喀斯木·买吐送面对镜头，桌上放着一本习近平的著作。</div><div id="attachment_672777" style="width: 510px" class="wp-caption aligncenter"><noscript><img aria-describedby="caption-attachment-672777" src="https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635862008597.png" alt="" width="500" class="size-full wp-image-672777" srcset="https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635862008597.png 642w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635862008597-300x291.png 300w" sizes="(max-width: 642px) 100vw, 642px"></noscript><img aria-describedby="caption-attachment-672777" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns=%22http://www.w3.org/2000/svg%22%20viewBox=%220%200%20500%20333.33333333333%22%3E%3C/svg%3E" data-src="https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635862008597.png" alt="" width="500" class="lazyload size-full wp-image-672777" data-srcset="https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635862008597.png 642w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635862008597-300x291.png 300w" data-sizes="(max-width: 642px) 100vw, 642px"><p id="caption-attachment-672777" class="wp-caption-text">来源：吾布力喀斯木·买吐送:一字一句写团结 / 人民日报 2017年7月16日（<a href="https://archive.ph/yPRV9">链接</a>）</p></div><p>最先作出这种表态的是维吾尔官员吾布力喀斯木·买吐送。在再教育运动开始时，他在于田县加依乡担任副书记，因为撰写了《致维吾尔族同胞觉醒书》而一夜成名。<span id="easy-footnote-280-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-280-672976" title="‘Flag waving in the wind: a profile on Obulqasim Mettursun, Deputy Party Secretary and County Magistrate of Awat County’ [迎风飘扬的旗—记新疆阿瓦提县委副书记、县长吾布力喀斯木·买吐送], Xinjiang Daily [新疆日报] via People’s Daily Online [人民网], 16 July 2018, online. "><sup>&nbsp;[280]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>根据他自己的说法，他写下这封公开信是受到当年春天新疆各地举行的一系列叫做“反恐维稳誓师大会”的军事展演的“启发”。他后来对媒体表示：“我们怎么能无动于衷呢？我要说话！”<span id="easy-footnote-281-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-281-672976" title="‘Obulqasim Mettursun: Emphasise “unity” with every word and every sentence’ [吾布力喀斯木·买吐送:一字一句写团结], People’s Daily [人民日报], 16 July 2017, online. "><sup>&nbsp;[281]&nbsp;</sup></a></span></p><p>买吐送在公开信中对党的政策表达感谢，并表示维吾尔人无法取得社会的“认同”和“包容”是因为“不少维吾尔人还没有清醒地认识到‘三股势力’对民族命运会造成怎样巨大的危害”，没能“亮剑”。他写道：</p><blockquote><p>“我们每一个维吾尔人都应更加旗帜鲜明地与‘三股势力’作斗争，都应更加主动地站在‘三股势力’的对立面。只有这样[……]维吾尔族的未来才会繁荣，维吾尔族才会真正地被大家认同、被大家包容。</p><p>维吾尔族同胞们，让我们觉醒吧！[……]用我们的勇气和担当赢得世人的谅解和尊重、用我们的贡献来获取曾被遗失的尊严[……]只有发自内心真诚的觉醒，才能让我们获得幸福的生活……”</p></blockquote><p>买吐送的汉语并不流利。<span id="easy-footnote-282-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-282-672976" title="‘Video: Obulqasim, 19th National People’s Congress delegate: We must unite and energise in order to seek development’ [微视频｜十九大代表吾布力喀斯木:团结鼓劲谋发展], Xigua Video [西瓜视频], 3 October 2017, online."><sup>&nbsp;[282]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>根据官方说法，他于2017年2月19日用维吾尔语写了这封信的初稿，并请人翻译成汉语。<span id="easy-footnote-283-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-283-672976" title="‘“Wake up call to fellow Uyghurs”: Hope to evoke the awakening of my fellow Uyghurs’ [《觉醒书》：希望能唤起维吾尔族同胞的觉醒], Sina News [新浪新闻], 31 March 2017, online. "><sup>&nbsp;[283]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>然后他得到该乡党委书记、汉人官员李仲刚的批准后，用了三天时间在该乡下属的12个村庄进行“宣讲”，向村民朗诵这封信，直到他的嗓子说不出话。<span id="easy-footnote-284-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-284-672976" title="Ibid. "><sup>&nbsp;[284]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>据国家媒体报道：“有的村民边听边抹眼泪，听完一场又去邻村再听一 场，‘乡长每句话都讲到了我们心坎里。’”<span id="easy-footnote-285-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-285-672976" title="‘Flag waving in the wind: a profile on Obulqasim Mettursun, Deputy Party Secretary and County Magistrate of Awat County’, Xinjiang Daily, 16 July 2017, online. "><sup>&nbsp;[285]&nbsp;</sup></a></span></p><div class="ar-caption">图26：吾布力喀斯木·买吐送对村民进行宣讲。</div><div id="attachment_672778" style="width: 510px" class="wp-caption aligncenter"><noscript><img
