class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-286-672976" title="‘Obulqasim Mettursun: Emphasise “unity” with every word and every sentence’, People’s Daily, 16 July 2017, online."><sup>&nbsp;[286]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>3月25日，新疆自治区党委要求在全疆开展“学习吾布力喀斯木·买吐送先进事迹”活动，并授予他“优秀共产党员”和“民族团结进步模范”称号。<span id="easy-footnote-287-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-287-672976" title="‘Learn from Obulqasim Mettursun’s example and experience’ [学习吾布力喀斯木•买吐送先进事迹心得体会], Xinjiang High People’s Court [新疆高级人民法院], 6 April 2017, online."><sup>&nbsp;[287]&nbsp;</sup></a></span></p><p>2017年4月左右，维吾尔和其他少数民族开始被投入再教育营中。4月6日，乌鲁木齐市新收犯监狱邀请买吐送进行在线“宣讲”，以消除犯人的“极端思想”。监狱在微信上宣传这一活动，称许多犯人表示要以买吐送为榜样，“学习他强烈的爱国热情”，“听党话感党恩跟党走”。<span id="easy-footnote-288-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-288-672976" title="‘Evoke inner awakening, eradicate extremist thoughts &amp;#8211; New Inmates Prison invites Obulqasim Mettursun to conduct remote propaganda lectures’ [唤起内心觉醒，去除极端思想—新收犯监狱邀请吾布力喀斯木•买吐送开展远程视频宣教活动], Xinjiang Prison [新疆监狱], 7 April 2017, online."><sup>&nbsp;[288]&nbsp;</sup></a></span></p><p>随着他的声音被放大，买吐送在事业上也见进展。5月18日，新疆两位高级官员——党委书记陈全国和时任组织部长马学军在乌鲁木齐会见了买吐送。<span id="easy-footnote-289-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-289-672976" title="‘Chen Quanguo meets with Obulqasim Mettursun’ [陈全国会见吾布力喀斯木•买吐送], Hejing County “Becoming Family” Program Leading Small Group on Hejing Zero Distance [民亲办微信公众号”和静零距离”], 19 May 2017, online."><sup>&nbsp;[289]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>陈全国高度评价买吐送“强烈的爱国热情”，并赠送了他一本《习近平谈治国理政》。<span id="easy-footnote-290-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-290-672976" title="Ibid. "><sup>&nbsp;[290]&nbsp;</sup></a></span></p><div class="ar-caption">图27：陈全国和马学军在乌鲁木齐会见买吐送。</div><div id="attachment_672779" style="width: 510px" class="wp-caption aligncenter"><noscript><img aria-describedby="caption-attachment-672779" src="https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635862106749.png" alt="" width="500" class="size-full wp-image-672779" srcset="https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635862106749.png 1204w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635862106749-300x192.png 300w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635862106749-1024x655.png 1024w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635862106749-768x491.png 768w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635862106749-1080x691.png 1080w" sizes="(max-width: 1204px) 100vw, 1204px"></noscript><img aria-describedby="caption-attachment-672779" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns=%22http://www.w3.org/2000/svg%22%20viewBox=%220%200%20500%20333.33333333333%22%3E%3C/svg%3E" data-src="https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635862106749.png" alt="" width="500" class="lazyload size-full wp-image-672779" data-srcset="https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635862106749.png 1204w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635862106749-300x192.png 300w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635862106749-1024x655.png 1024w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635862106749-768x491.png 768w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635862106749-1080x691.png 1080w" data-sizes="(max-width: 1204px) 100vw, 1204px"><p id="caption-attachment-672779" class="wp-caption-text">来源：陈全国在会见吾布力喀斯木·买吐送 / 乌鲁木齐市政府网站 2017年5月19日（<a href="https://archive.ph/wip/uH1MG">链接</a>）</p></div><p>到了8月，新疆党委再次号召向买吐送学习，<span id="easy-footnote-291-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-291-672976" title="‘Notes from the advancement ceremony on “Learn from Comrade Obulkasim Mettursun to speak up and brandish the sword”’ [向吾布力喀斯木•买吐送同志学习发声亮剑推进会侧记及综述], Kashgar Daily on WeChat [喀什日报微信公众号“喀什零距离”], 4 August 2017, online. "><sup>&nbsp;[291]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>新疆的每个人——从党的干部到普通公民，都被号召以他为榜样。买吐送开始成为国家媒体大力报道的对象。在访谈中，他有时把习近平的书拿在手中，发誓要“亮剑绝杀敌人”；<span id="easy-footnote-292-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-292-672976" title="282   ‘Learn from Comrade Obulqasim Mettursun, promote “Speak Up and Brandish the Sword” activities’, Kashgar Daily,<br />4 August 2017, online; ‘Xinjiang holds advancement meeting on “Learn from Comrade Mattersun to speak up and brandish the sword”’ [自治区召开向吾布力喀斯木·买吐送同志学习发声亮剑推进会], CCP Xinjiang Commission for Discipline Inspection [中共新疆维吾尔自治区纪律检查委员会], 16 August 2017, online."><sup>&nbsp;[292]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>有时则坐在办公室里，习近平的书摆在他的桌子上。<span id="easy-footnote-293-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-293-672976" title="‘Obulqasim Mettursun: Emphasise “unity” with every word and every sentence’, People’s Daily, 16 July 2017, online. "><sup>&nbsp;[293]&nbsp;</sup></a></span></p><p>2017年8月，在发表《致维吾尔族同胞觉醒书》六个月后，买吐送被提拔为阿瓦提县党委副书记。<span id="easy-footnote-294-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-294-672976" title="‘Flag waving in the wind: a profile on Obulqasim Mettursun, Deputy Party Secretary and County Magistrate of Awat County’, Xinjiang Daily, 16 July 2017, online. "><sup>&nbsp;[294]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>10月，他作为新疆的代表到北京参加中共十九大。<span id="easy-footnote-295-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-295-672976" title="‘Delegate Obulkasim Mettursun: From “becoming rich” to “becoming strong”’ [吾布力喀斯木·买吐送代表：从‘富起来’到‘强起来’], People’s Daily Online [人民网], 22 October 2017, online. "><sup>&nbsp;[295]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>在成为县级官员的一年内，买吐送撰写了17份关于“发声亮剑”的新文稿，并在新疆巡回举办了约130场宣传讲座。<span id="easy-footnote-296-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-296-672976" title=" ‘Flag waving in the wind: a profile on Obulqasim Mettursun, Deputy Party Secretary and County Magistrate of Awat County’, Xinjiang Daily, 16 July 2017, online."><sup>&nbsp;[296]&nbsp;</sup></a></span></p><p>尽管买吐送名气不减，但和大多数维吾尔官员一样，他的官职至今仍是二把手。2021年，他出席了中央宣传部举行的新闻发布会，向外国记者表示在新疆“老百姓的腰包比以前越来越鼓了，脸上的幸福笑容越来越美了”。<span id="easy-footnote-297-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-297-672976" title="‘Central Propaganda Department holds foreign press conference on “The Chinese nation-race is one close family, building the China dream together sharing the same heart”’ [中共中央宣传部就‘中华民族一家亲，同心共筑中国梦’举行中外记者见面会], chinanews.com [中国网], 27 July 2021, online. "><sup>&nbsp;[297]&nbsp;</sup></a></span></p><h2>第七章：“没有与稳定无关的部门”</h2><p>2014年8月，时任新疆自治区书记张春贤写道：“牢固树立没有与稳定无关的地方、无关的部门、无关的人的观念。”<span id="easy-footnote-298-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-298-672976" title="Zhang Chunxian, ‘Strive to write the new chapter of long-term stable rule and social stability in Xinjiang’ [张春贤：奋力谱写新疆社会稳定和长治久安新篇章], People’s Daily Online [人民网], 13 January 2014, online."><sup>&nbsp;[298]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>在新疆的运动中，几乎没有哪个部门或官员能逃脱高度政治化的“维稳”职责。有时，压迫性政策是由听起来最无辜、最不起眼的政府机构执行的。例如，喀什市林业局曾在一年的时间里负责管理喀什再教育营的账目。<span id="easy-footnote-299-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-299-672976" title="Release of the 2018 Xinjiang Kashgar Forestry Bureau’s budget’ [新疆维吾尔自治区喀什市林业局 2018年部门预算公开], online. "><sup>&nbsp;[299]&nbsp;</sup></a></span></p><p>本章对反恐和再教育运动的五个重要方面——宣传、再教育营、“访惠聚”、强迫劳动和人口控制——作出概述，并指出了每一方面所涉及的行政机构。作者们也将这些行政结构以交互式结构图的形式绘制在了“<a href="https://xjdp.aspi.org.au/chart" title="新疆数据项目">新疆数据项目</a>”网站上。</p><div class="ar-caption">图28：从2014年至今参与过新疆治理的党政军以及混合实体的组织结构图（截图）</div><div id="attachment_672780" style="width: 510px" class="wp-caption aligncenter"><noscript><img aria-describedby="caption-attachment-672780" src="https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635862279069.png" alt="" width="500" class="size-full wp-image-672780" srcset="https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635862279069.png 1206w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635862279069-300x158.png 300w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635862279069-1024x538.png 1024w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635862279069-768x404.png 768w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635862279069-1080x568.png 1080w" sizes="(max-width: 1206px) 100vw, 1206px"></noscript><img aria-describedby="caption-attachment-672780" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns=%22http://www.w3.org/2000/svg%22%20viewBox=%220%200%20500%20333.33333333333%22%3E%3C/svg%3E" data-src="https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635862279069.png" alt="" width="500" class="lazyload size-full wp-image-672780" data-srcset="https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635862279069.png 1206w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635862279069-300x158.png 300w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635862279069-1024x538.png 1024w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635862279069-768x404.png 768w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635862279069-1080x568.png 1080w" data-sizes="(max-width: 1206px) 100vw, 1206px"><p id="caption-attachment-672780" class="wp-caption-text">来源：ASPI</p></div><h4>宣传</h4><p>与中国其他地方相比，新疆的宣传工作更加密集、无处不在，并带有强烈的种族色彩。本章节按照时间顺序概述新疆的宣传工作政策，其中包括公开的效忠宣誓、“宣讲”、祝愿习近平健康的口号，以及针对“极端分子”和“两面人”的揭批大会。如第二章所述，这些政治仪式具有毛泽东时代大规模政治运动的特征。</p><p>2014年5月28日，在反恐运动开启四天后，北京召开了一场关于新疆工作的高层会议。习近平在会议期间指示，为了实现新疆的稳定和党的控制，一个关键措施是“要大力选拔对党忠诚、关键时刻敢于发声亮剑、有较强群众工作能力和应对突发事件、驾驭复杂局面能力的干部”。<span id="easy-footnote-300-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-300-672976" title="‘Xi Jinping: Must firmly establish the correct national and ethnic identity among the masses of all ethnicities’ (习近平: 要在各族群众中牢固树立正确的祖国观、民族观), Xinhua Net (新华网), 29 May 2014, online."><sup>&nbsp;[300]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>在这个时间点上，所谓“亮剑”似乎是一种修辞手法，比喻坚定地对党表达忠诚，并准备好通过斗争来捍卫党。<span id="easy-footnote-301-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-301-672976" title="307   ‘Zhang Chunxian discussing counter-terrorism: Cadres of all ethnicities must dare to “speak up and brandish the sword” at the first moment’ [张春贤谈反恐：各族干部要第一时间敢于发声亮剑], Tianshan News [天山网] via chinanews.com [中国新闻网], 9 February 2014, online; ‘Social scientists in Xinjiang support the call to “speak up and brandish the sword” in our struggle against religious extremism’ [新疆社科界人士：主动发声‘亮剑，’   反对宗教极端主义], Tianshan News [天山网] via Sina News [新浪新闻], 25 September 2013, online."><sup>&nbsp;[301]&nbsp;</sup></a></span></p><div class="ar-caption">图29：2017年，和田地区教师集体“发声亮剑”。</div><div id="attachment_672781" style="width: 510px" class="wp-caption aligncenter"><noscript><img aria-describedby="caption-attachment-672781" src="https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635862356795.png" alt="" width="500" class="size-full wp-image-672781" https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635862356795-1024x620.png 1024w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635862356795-768x465.png 768w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635862356795-1080x654.png 1080w" sizes="(max-width: 1202px) 100vw, 1202px"></noscript><img aria-describedby="caption-attachment-672781" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns=%22http://www.w3.org/2000/svg%22%20viewBox=%220%200%20500%20333.33333333333%22%3E%3C/svg%3E" data-src="https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635862356795.png" alt="" width="500" class="lazyload size-full wp-image-672781" data-srcset="https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635862356795.png 1202w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635862356795-300x182.png 300w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635862356795-1024x620.png 1024w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635862356795-768x465.png 768w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635862356795-1080x654.png 1080w" data-sizes="(max-width: 1202px) 100vw, 1202px"><p id="caption-attachment-672781" class="wp-caption-text">来源：和田地区万名教师学生集体发声亮剑 发出正义最强音 誓与“三股势力”和“两面人”斗争到底 / 和田政务在线 2017年6月27日（<a href="https://freewechat.com/a/MzAxNTc5MzQxMw==/2651114577/4">链接</a>）</p></div><p>“发声亮剑”这个修辞手法很快就演变成了新疆特有的政治仪式。在北京那场新疆工作会召开九天后，且末县约有一万人公开承诺对“恐怖犯罪亮剑”。<span id="easy-footnote-302-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-302-672976" title="Tao Shuanke [陶拴科], ‘Ten thousand masses pledge to “brandish the sword” against terror in Cherchen County, Xinjiang [Gallery]’ [新疆且末县万名群众宣誓，向恐怖犯罪“亮剑”[组图]], Photo China [图片中国], 6 June 2014, online."><sup>&nbsp;[302]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>据报道，2014年7月，莎车县一群维吾尔人与大量军警人员发生暴力冲突后，<span id="easy-footnote-303-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-303-672976" title="The Chinese party-state called the incident a terrorist attack, while Uyghur groups said it was resistance following the killing of a Uyghur family over a headscarf check. Andrew Jacobs, ‘After deadly clash, China and Uighurs disagree on events that led to violence’, The New York Times, 30 July 2014, online. "><sup>&nbsp;[303]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>当地官员在村委会院内振臂高呼“坚决维护国家统一！”“坚决维护法律尊严！”大约130名村级官员共同签署公开信，谴责这一暴力袭击。<span id="easy-footnote-304-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-304-672976" title="‘Cadres and masses of all ethnicities in Yarkant, Xinjiang “speak up and brandish the sword”, declare war on violent terrorists’ [新疆莎车各族干部群众发声亮剑向暴恐分子宣战], Ürümqi Evening News [乌鲁木齐晚报] via chinanews. com [中国新闻网], 8 August 2014, online."><sup>&nbsp;[304]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>此后，官员、平民、<span id="easy-footnote-305-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-305-672976" title="‘Cadres and masses of all ethnicities in Ürümqi “speak up and brandish the sword”: Joint defence to crack down on violence and terrorism’ [乌鲁木齐各族干部群众发声亮剑：联防联保打击暴恐], Tianshan News [天山网] via People’s Daily Online [人民网], 7 August 2014, online. "><sup>&nbsp;[305]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>宗教领袖、<span id="easy-footnote-306-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-306-672976" title="Mihrigul Wu [米日古力·吾], ‘Religious figures in Xinjiang “speak up and brandish the sword”’ [新疆宗教界人士发声亮剑], Xinjiang News [新疆网], 18 April 2017, online. "><sup>&nbsp;[306]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>企业家、<span id="easy-footnote-307-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-307-672976" title=" ‘Commentary: “Speak up and brandish the sword” demonstrates the sense of responsibility of ethnic minority enterprises’ [评论：发声亮剑彰显民族企业的责任与担当], Private Corporates’ Social Responsibility Net [民营企业社会责任网], 8 July 2014, online."><sup>&nbsp;[307]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>艺术工作者<span id="easy-footnote-308-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-308-672976" title="Zhu Kaili [朱凯莉], Pang Xuefang [庞雪芳], ‘Cultural workers of Xinjiang “speak up and brandish the sword”: Don’t let dark clouds obscure the bright moon’ [新疆文化工作者发声亮剑：不让乌云遮明月], Tianshan News [天山网] via Sina News [新浪新闻], 14 August 2014, online."><sup>&nbsp;[308]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>和残疾人<span id="easy-footnote-309-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-309-672976" title="Mihrigul Wu, Fang Feiyang [方菲洋], ‘Representatives of the disabled people in Xinjiang “speak up and brandish the sword”, expressing determination to resolutely resist religious extremist thoughts’ [新疆残疾人代表发声亮剑,坚决抵制宗教极端思想], Xinjiang Daily [新疆日报], 29 August 2014, online. "><sup>&nbsp;[309]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>都签署了类似的承诺书，来“发声亮剑”。</p><p>“发声亮剑”仪式很快变得十分普遍。参与者以站立的姿势举起拳头呈宣誓状，发声谴责“宗教极端主义”，赞扬党和党的政策。<span id="easy-footnote-310-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-310-672976" title=" ‘At the regional grassroots propaganda work and winter propaganda lecture mobilization meeting, Zhang Chunxian orders to be a politically determined leader, a fighter who dares to speak up and can speak up, and a caring person to all ethnicities’ [张春贤在自治区基层宣传工作暨冬季大宣讲动员会议上要求做政治坚定的引领者敢讲会讲的战斗员各族群众的贴心人], Huaxia News [华夏经纬网], 5 January 2016, online; ‘“We love listening to propaganda lectures like this!”: Tens of thousands of people attend large-scale public propaganda lectures’ [【冬季万人大宣讲】这样的宣讲，我们很爱听!], Aksu City Media Communication Centre on WeChat [阿克苏市融媒体中心腾讯微信公众账号阿克苏市零距离], 10 January 2019, online. "><sup>&nbsp;[310]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>参与者还被要求在巨大的宣传横幅上签名，并“郑重承诺感党恩、听党话、跟党走”。<span id="easy-footnote-311-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-311-672976" title="‘A hundred women participate in “speak up and brandish the sword”, vowing to be pretty women’ [百名妇女发声亮剑 做靓丽女性], Global Times [环球网], 11 April 2017, online; ‘More than one hundred women of all ethnic groups in Tokkuztara speak up and brandish the sword’ [巩留百余名各族妇女发声亮剑], Xinjiang Ili Kazakh Autonomous Prefecture People’s Government [新疆伊犁哈萨克自治州人民政府], 28 April 2017, online."><sup>&nbsp;[311]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>一些官员声称，这些活动可以治愈“极端主义”的疾病，改善群众的心理健康。<span id="easy-footnote-312-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-312-672976" title="Pan Congwu, ‘Xinjiang “de-extremification” propaganda lecture group’, China Peace, 19 May 2016, online. "><sup>&nbsp;[312]&nbsp;</sup></a></span></p><div class="ar-caption">图30：新疆图木舒克市女性“发声亮剑”仪式。</div><div id="attachment_672782" style="width: 510px" class="wp-caption aligncenter"><noscript><img aria-describedby="caption-attachment-672782" src="https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635862412258.png" alt="" width="500" class="size-full wp-image-672782" srcset="https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635862412258.png 1188w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635862412258-300x199.png 300w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635862412258-1024x681.png 1024w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635862412258-768x511.png 768w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635862412258-1080x718.png 1080w" sizes="(max-width: 1188px) 100vw, 1188px"></noscript><img aria-describedby="caption-attachment-672782" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns=%22http://www.w3.org/2000/svg%22%20viewBox=%220%200%20500%20333.33333333333%22%3E%3C/svg%3E" data-src="https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635862412258.png" alt="" width="500" class="lazyload size-full wp-image-672782" data-srcset="https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635862412258.png 1188w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635862412258-300x199.png 300w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635862412258-1024x681.png 1024w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635862412258-768x511.png 768w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635862412258-1080x718.png 1080w" data-sizes="(max-width: 1188px) 100vw, 1188px"><p id="caption-attachment-672782" class="wp-caption-text">来源：大宣讲：师市“大揭批大声讨大宣讲”系列活动精彩图集 / 市党委宣传部 2017年4月28日（<a href="https://archive.ph/GeqXA">链接</a>）</p></div><p>2014年8月26日，新疆组织部在一份公开工作报告中说，该部将提拔六名带头在公开场合或媒体上批评“三股势力”的少数民族官员，<span id="easy-footnote-313-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-313-672976" title="‘Xinjiang: Implement stricter requirements and strengthen daily management and supervision of cadres’, Central Organisation Department, 26 August 2014, online."><sup>&nbsp;[313]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>并“对政治上不够坚强、关键时刻不敢发声亮剑的65名考察对象，取消提名资格”。<span id="easy-footnote-314-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-314-672976" title="Ibid. "><sup>&nbsp;[314]&nbsp;</sup></a></span></p><p>四个月后，在时任新疆党委书记张春贤的指示下，宣传部准备了讲课提纲并组织了“宣讲团”。<span id="easy-footnote-315-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-315-672976" title="‘Propaganda lecture activities in Xinjiang are in full swing’ [新疆宣讲活动火热展开], State Council Information Office [国务院新闻办公室], 31 December 2014, online. "><sup>&nbsp;[315]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>“宣讲”指的是一组讲演者用数周或数月时间在村庄和乡镇的学校或体育场巡回讲演，听众从几十到上万人不等。<span id="easy-footnote-316-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-316-672976" title="‘Ten thousand people attended public propaganda lectures in Aksu, Xinjiang: Speeches facilitate confidence, unity and harmony’ [新疆阿克苏万人大宣讲：讲出信心讲出团结讲出和谐], Guangming Daily [光明日报] via People’s Daily Online [人民网], 8 April 2019, online; ‘”De-extremification” and rule by law propaganda lectures covered the urban and rural areas of Kashgar’ [“去极端化”法制宣讲覆盖喀什城乡], Kashgar Zero Distance [喀什零距离], 24 February 2014, online.  / ‘Xinjiang launches “de-extremification” propaganda lecture educational activities’ [自治区“去极端化”系列宣讲教育活动启动], Xinjiang Economics News [新疆经济报] via Xinjiang United Front Work Department [新疆统一战线工作<br />部], 21 March 2017, online; Pang Congwu, ‘Xinjiang’s “de-extremification” propaganda lecture group: Sowing the seeds of harmony and stability among the hearts of the masses’ [新疆‘去极端化’宣讲团：把和谐稳定种子播撒群众心中], China Peace [长安网], 19 May 2016, online."><sup>&nbsp;[316]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>演讲者通常包括党和政府官员、执法人员、宗教领袖、教师、被拘留过的人、心理咨询师，<span id="easy-footnote-317-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-317-672976" title="Pang Congwu, ‘Xinjiang’s “de-extremification” propaganda lecture group: sowing the seeds of harmony and stability among the hearts of the masses’, China Peace, 19 May 2016, online."><sup>&nbsp;[317]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>以及被称为“草根宣讲员”的普通公民。<span id="easy-footnote-318-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-318-672976" title="‘Kizilsu launches “de-extremification” winter public propaganda lecture activities’ [克州开展“去极端化” 冬季大宣讲活动], Xinjiang People’s Government [新疆人民政府], 19 November 2014, online; Wang Se, ‘Ten thousand people attended public propaganda lectures in Aksu’, Guangming Daily, 8 April 2019, online."><sup>&nbsp;[318]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>在再教育运动期间，司法厅和其下的“促进和谐预防犯罪宣讲办公室”在动员和组织“宣讲团”方面发挥了主导作用。<span id="easy-footnote-319-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-319-672976" title="322   Pang Congwu, ‘Xinjiang’s “de-extremification” propaganda lecture group: Sowing the seeds of harmony and stability among the hearts of the masses’, China Peace, 19 May 2016, online; ‘Launch of “de-extremification” propaganda lecture’, Xinjiang United Front Work Department, 21 March 2017, online; ‘Xinjiang appoints new officials Xie Huiqing, Li Wei, Abduwahid Seydiwaqqas, He Yuhong’ [新疆任命谢惠青、李伟、阿布都瓦依提·赛迪瓦卡斯、何玉红职务], China Economics News Online [中国经济网], 26 July 2016, online; Zhang Sifu [张世福], ‘Using emotional appeals to reach the hearts and minds of the masses, use reasoning to sooth the emotions of the masses’ [用情感敲开心灵大门，用说理舒缓群众情绪], Baijiahao [百家号], 14 April 2017, online. "><sup>&nbsp;[319]&nbsp;</sup></a></span></p><div class="ar-caption"> 图31：2017年，喀什市对草根宣讲员进行培训。</div><div id="attachment_672783" style="width: 510px" class="wp-caption aligncenter"><noscript><img aria-describedby="caption-attachment-672783" src="https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635862472112.png" alt="" width="500" class="size-full wp-image-672783" srcset="https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635862472112.png 838w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635862472112-300x276.png 300w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635862472112-768x706.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 838px) 100vw, 838px"></noscript><img aria-describedby="caption-attachment-672783" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns=%22http://www.w3.org/2000/svg%22%20viewBox=%220%200%20500%20333.33333333333%22%3E%3C/svg%3E" data-src="https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635862472112.png" alt="" width="500" class="lazyload size-full wp-image-672783" data-srcset="https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635862472112.png 838w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635862472112-300x276.png 300w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635862472112-768x706.png 768w" data-sizes="(max-width: 838px) 100vw, 838px"><p id="caption-attachment-672783" class="wp-caption-text">来源：喀什市对草根宣讲员进行党的十九大精神专题培训 / 喀什市微信公众号（喀什零距离）2017年11月16日（<a href="https://freewechat.com/a/MzA4NTMzOTE2MA==/2650115068/5">链接</a>）</p></div><p>2017年4月，新疆自治区统战部在乌鲁木齐举办了一系列“三爱、三反”研讨会，持续了十多天，有近千名来自新疆社会各界的代表参加。<span id="easy-footnote-320-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-320-672976" title="Wang Yayun [王亚芸], ‘General mobilisation for all ethnicities and all walks of life speak up and brandish swords to contribute to the the realization of the overall goals &amp;#8211; overview of the “three loves, three oppositions” themed speak up and brandish swords activities’ [各族各界发声亮剑总动员，为实现总目标贡献力量—自治区‘三爱三反’发声亮剑系列活动综述], Central United Front Work Department [中央统战部], 3 March 2017, online."><sup>&nbsp;[320]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>“三爱、三反”是来自习近平名言的一句口号，全称是“热爱党、热爱祖国、热爱中华民族大家庭，反分裂、反极端、反暴力”。<span id="easy-footnote-321-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-321-672976" title="Ibid. "><sup>&nbsp;[321]&nbsp;</sup></a></span></p><p>“三爱、三反”很快成为新疆各地宣讲和亮剑仪式的主题，<span id="easy-footnote-322-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-322-672976" title="‘“Three gratitudes, three wishes” activities lead herdsmen, farmers and party members in Uchturpan County to demonstrate loyalty’ [“三感恩,三祝愿”引领乌什农牧民党员践忠诚], Xinjiang Daily [新疆日报] via Tianshan News [天山网], 16 June 2017, online; ‘Burchin County: “Three gratitudes, three wishes” themed public lectures during flag raising ceremony on Monday, stirring patriotic feelings’ [布尔津：周一升国旗‘三感恩，三祝愿’主题宣讲,激发爱国情], Central People’s Government [中央人民政府], 6 June 2017, online; ‘Ili prefecture supply and marketing system launches “three loves, three oppositions” and “three gratitudes, three wishes” themed “speak up and brandish the sword” activities’ [伊犁州供销系统开展 ‘三爱三反’‘三感恩三祝愿’主题发声亮剑活动], Xinjiang Supply and Marketing Cooperative [新疆供销社], 27 June 2017, online; Li Yongfu [李永福], ‘“Three loves, three oppositions, three gratitudes, three wishes” propaganda lectures and public pledge activities inspire patriotism among villagers’ [“三爱三反三祝愿”宣讲签名活动激发村民爱国热情], Xinjiang Livelihood News [新疆民生网], 23 May 2017, online; ‘Nilqa County women’s federation held embroidery skills competition and “becoming family beautiful projects” themed clothing display’ [尼勒克县妇联举办‘刺绣技能竞赛’暨‘靓丽工程•民族团结一家亲’服装展示活动], Voices of the Women of Ili [伊犁女声], 25 May 2017, online."><sup>&nbsp;[322]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>并被扩展为“三爱、三反、三感恩、三祝愿”。在这些仪式上，常被诵读的“三感恩”和“三祝愿”内容如下：</p><blockquote><p>感恩伟大祖国，感恩中国共产党，感恩习近平总书记；祝愿伟大祖国繁荣昌盛，祝愿习近平总书记身体健康，祝愿各族人民团结和谐。<span id="easy-footnote-323-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-323-672976" title="‘“Three gratitudes, three wishes” activities’, Xinjiang Daily, 16 June 2017, online. "><sup>&nbsp;[323]&nbsp;</sup></a></span></p></blockquote><p>升旗仪式、宣讲和发声亮剑经常合并进行，随后在国家媒体上公开，媒体常报道参与者在仪式上情绪激动、不禁流泪。<span id="easy-footnote-324-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-324-672976" title="Xinjiang launches “de-extremification” propaganda lecture educational activities’, Xinjiang Economics News, 31 March 2017, online; ‘[Big propaganda lecture] This ‘de-extremification’ education method is in touch with the masses’ [大宣讲] 这样的“去极端化”教育方式接地气], Niye Zero Distance [民丰零距离] via Sohu News [搜狐新闻], 12 September 2017, online; Ma Linrong [马琳荣], Xi Xiaoyu [席晓宇], ’A hundred women in Ushtala township in Hoshut Township deeply moved by listening to propaganda lectures’ [新疆和硕县：乌什塔拉乡百名妇女聆听宣讲讲到心坎里], Yaxin News [亚心网] via Sina News [新浪新闻], 29 November 2017, online; ‘Ghulja City drums up strong “de-extremification” propaganda education atmosphere’ [伊宁市营造‘去极端化’宣传教育浓厚氛围], Yaxin News [亚心网] via China Xinjiang [中国新疆], 21 January 2015, online."><sup>&nbsp;[324]&nbsp;</sup></a></span></p><p>在新疆的两次运动中，当局还推广了名为“大声讨、大揭批”的批斗会。这些仪式涉及到公开谴责那些被指控为“两面人”的个人，<span id="easy-footnote-325-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-325-672976" title="‘Chapchal Township launches “the big denounce, expose and criticise” activities’ [察布查尔镇开展‘大声讨大揭批’活动], Chapchal Town Bulletin [察布查尔镇微讯], 12 April 2017, online; ‘Using hard measures to cure a lack of discipline and gather [our] strength to build the foundation: the rehabilitation of weak village [community] party committee in Ili Kazakh Prefecture, Xinjiang’ [硬招治软散,聚力强基石—新疆伊犁州软弱涣散村（社区）党组织如期“摘帽”], CCP Members Net [共产党员网], 9 January 2017, online; ‘Improve ideological immunity, educate and guide the masses, Ichyan Village carries out “big denounce, expose and criticise” activities’ [提高思想免疫力教育引导群众依其央村开展‘大宣讲大揭批大声讨大反思’活动], FX361, 13 September 2018, online. "><sup>&nbsp;[325]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>并呼吁公众举报身边的“两面人”。<span id="easy-footnote-326-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-326-672976" title="Wang Zhenfei [王振飞], ‘Ergon Village in Qingshuihe Township holds “expose and criticise” mass meeting’ [清水河镇二宫村召开群众揭批大会], Xinjiang Korgas County People’s Government [新疆霍城县人民政府], 30 March 2017, online. "><sup>&nbsp;[326]&nbsp;</sup></a></span></p><div class="ar-caption"> 图32：2018年，巴楚镇召开“大宣讲、大揭批、大声讨，大反思”活动。</div><div id="attachment_672784" style="width: 510px" class="wp-caption aligncenter"><noscript><img aria-describedby="caption-attachment-672784" src="https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635862569756.png" alt="" width="500" class="size-full https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635862569756-1024x490.png 1024w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635862569756-768x367.png 768w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635862569756-1080x516.png 1080w" data-sizes="(max-width: 1188px) 100vw, 1188px"><p id="caption-attachment-672784" class="wp-caption-text">来源：巴楚镇召开“大宣讲、大揭批、大声讨，大反思”活动暨发声亮剑大会现场推进会 / 巴楚靓丽巾帼（微信公众号） 2018年3月21日（<a href="https://www.documentcloud.org/documents/21079974-ba-chu-zhen-zhao-kai-da-xuan-jiang-da-jie-pi-da-sheng-tao-da-fan-si-huo-dong-ji-fa-sheng-liang-jian-da-hui-xian-chang-tui-jin-hui-screencapture-mp-weixin-qq-s-2021-10-06-02_12_47">链接</a>）</p></div><p>在基层，“访惠聚”工作队、驻村管寺管委会和居/村委会也组织规模较小的宣讲活动。<span id="easy-footnote-327-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-327-672976" title="Mu Min [牟敏], ‘Communities set up grassroots propaganda lecture groups to come up with different ways to promote the spirit of the 19th National People’s Congress’ [社区成立基层宣讲团，形式多样宣传十九大精神], Xinjiang News [ 新疆网], 13 November 2017, online; ‘“Big propaganda lecture, expose, criticise, denounce and reflect” to “speak up and brandish the sword” activities’ [‘大宣讲、大揭批、大声讨、大反思’ 发声亮剑活动], Sound of Irtysh River [额河水之声], 9 May 2018, online<br />"><sup>&nbsp;[327]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>据报道，在2015年至2020年期间，有1.2万个“访惠聚”工作队和110万名官员在新疆南部地区深入居民家中进行“去极端化”宣讲。<span id="easy-footnote-328-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-328-672976" title="Sui Yunyan [隋云雁], ‘“7th Five-year Plan” legal education &amp;#8211; laid firm foundation for ruling Xinjiang in accordance with law’ [‘七五’普法：为依法治疆奠定坚实基础], Xinjiang Daily [新疆日报], 26 December 2020, online. "><sup>&nbsp;[328]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>政府机构（如检察院或法院）、居/村委会干部、全国妇女联合会地方分会和私营企业都组织过“发声亮剑”仪式。<span id="easy-footnote-329-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-329-672976" title="‘Derui Company personnel joins “speak up and brandish the sword” activities’ [德瑞公司发声亮剑专题], Derui Hotel Management Company [德瑞酒店管理公司], 24 October 2018, online. "><sup>&nbsp;[329]&nbsp;</sup></a></span></p><h4>再教育营</h4><p>研究人员发现，在再教育运动期间，拘留维吾尔人和其他少数民族的理由非常广泛，包括宗教表达（斋戒、祈祷、戴头巾或留胡子）、<span id="easy-footnote-330-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-330-672976" title="322   ‘“Break their lineage, break their roots”: China’s crimes against humanity targeting Uyghurs and other Turkic Muslims’, Human Rights Watch, 19 April 2021, online. "><sup>&nbsp;[330]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>境外联系（过去曾去过海外、与国外的人有联系或申请护照）、<span id="easy-footnote-331-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-331-672976" title="Ibid. "><sup>&nbsp;[331]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>触碰到未经批准的信息（使用“快牙”或WhatsApp）或生育太多孩子。<span id="easy-footnote-332-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-332-672976" title="Matthew Hill, David Campanale, Joel Gunter, ‘“Their goal is to destroy everyone”: Uighur camp detainees allege systematic rape’, BBC News, 2 February 2020, online. "><sup>&nbsp;[332]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>如本报告第四章所述，有时候，拘留一个人并不一定需要理由。</p><div class="ar-caption"> 图33：从2017年到2020年9月，ASPI研究人员在新疆发现了388个新建或扩建的拘留设施。</div><div id="attachment_672785" style="width: 510px" class="wp-caption aligncenter"><noscript><img aria-describedby="caption-attachment-672785" src="https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635862749733.png" alt="" width="500" 1210px) 100vw, 1210px"></noscript><img aria-describedby="caption-attachment-672785" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns=%22http://www.w3.org/2000/svg%22%20viewBox=%220%200%20500%20333.33333333333%22%3E%3C/svg%3E" data-src="https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635862749733.png" alt="" width="500" class="lazyload size-full wp-image-672785" data-srcset="https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635862749733.png 1210w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635862749733-300x229.png 300w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635862749733-1024x780.png 1024w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635862749733-768x585.png 768w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635862749733-1080x823.png 1080w" data-sizes="(max-width: 1210px) 100vw, 1210px"><p id="caption-attachment-672785" class="wp-caption-text">来源：内森·鲁瑟（Nathan Ruser） / ASPI新疆拘留设施数据 2020年9月24日（<a href="https://xjdp.aspi.org.au/map/">链接</a>）<br></p></div><p>2015年，新疆的一些党政机关开始起草“去极端化”规定，涉及的部门包括政法委、公安厅、司法厅等等。<span id="easy-footnote-333-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-333-672976" title="Memeteli Tursun [麦麦提艾力·吐尔孙], ‘Birth of the Xinjiang de-extremification regulations’ [自治区去极端化条例诞生记], China Academic Journal Electronic Publishing House, 5 May 2017, online. "><sup>&nbsp;[333]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>经中央批准，《新疆维吾尔自治区去极端化条例》于2017年3月29日颁布。2018年10月，当局修订了该条例，追溯性地为再教育拘留设施提供合法性。<span id="easy-footnote-334-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-334-672976" title="Liu Caiyu, Liu Xuanzun, ‘Xinjiang revises its anti-extremism regulation’, Global Times, 10 October 2018, online; Jeremy Daum, ‘Explainer on Xinjiang regulations’, China Law Translate, 11 October 2018, online. "><sup>&nbsp;[334]&nbsp;</sup></a></span></p><p>如本报告第三章所述，“三位一体”机制直接负责把维吾尔人移交给再教育营。自2018年起，新疆县级和地级的再教育营由教培局正式管理。<span id="easy-footnote-335-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-335-672976" title="‘Official telegram’, Xinjiang PLAC via ICIJ, online; ‘Public statement on Fukang City Vocational Education and Training Service Management Bureau’s 2018 departmental budget, as well as the “three public expenditures” budget’ [阜康市职业技能教育培训服务管理局 2018 年部门预算及‘三公’经费预算: 信息公开报告], online; ‘Notice on the approval to the adjustments of the 2018 budget revenue and expenditures of Pichan County’ [关于批准调整鄯善县2018年财政预算收支的通知], Pichan County People’s Congress [鄯善县人民代表大会], 2018, online."><sup>&nbsp;[335]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>监督教培局的是“职业技能教育培训领导小组”，该小组由当地党委书记领导，由公安局、司法局、教育局和卫健委的官员组成。<span id="easy-footnote-336-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-336-672976" title="‘Official telegram’, Xinjiang PLAC via ICIJ, 2017, online. "><sup>&nbsp;[336]&nbsp;</sup></a></span></p><p>在喀什市，ASPI的研究人员发现，至少有五个再教育营是2017年后建造或扩建的。<span id="easy-footnote-337-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-337-672976" title="The Xinjiang Data Project, ASPI, Canberra, online."><sup>&nbsp;[337]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>2017年喀什新建拘留设施的预算是975万人民币（300万美元）。在教培局成立之前，这笔预算由林业局负责。<span id="easy-footnote-338-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-338-672976" title="‘Release of the 2018 Xinjiang Kashgar Forestry Bureau’s budget’ [新疆维吾尔自治区喀什市林业局 2018年部门预算公开], online."><sup>&nbsp;[338]&nbsp;</sup></a></span></p><p>被拘留者必须学习各种课程并通过考试，包括政治思想和汉语。当地教育局负责出考题、评分。<span id="easy-footnote-339-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-339-672976" title="‘Official telegram’, Xinjiang PLAC via ICIJ, 2017, online."><sup>&nbsp;[339]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>理论上，被拘留者的考试成绩是释放他们的主要标准之一。<span id="easy-footnote-340-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-340-672976" title="‘Official telegram’, Xinjiang PLAC via ICIJ, 2017, online."><sup>&nbsp;[340]&nbsp;</sup></a></span></p><div class="ar-caption">图34：再教育营“营员”身着传统汉服在一座村庄表演。</div><div id="attachment_672786" style="width: 510px" class="wp-caption aligncenter"><noscript><img aria-describedby="caption-attachment-672786" src="https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635862908390.png" alt="" width="500" class="size-full wp-image-672786" srcset="https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635862908390.png 1206w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635862908390-300x199.png 300w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635862908390-1024x679.png 1024w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635862908390-768x509.png 768w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635862908390-1080x716.png 1080w" sizes="(max-width: 1206px) 100vw, 1206px"></noscript><img aria-describedby="caption-attachment-672786" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns=%22http://www.w3.org/2000/svg%22%20viewBox=%220%200%20500%20333.33333333333%22%3E%3C/svg%3E" data-src="https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635862908390.png" alt="" width="500" class="lazyload size-full wp-image-672786" data-srcset="https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635862908390.png 1206w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635862908390-300x199.png 300w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635862908390-1024x679.png 1024w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635862908390-768x509.png 768w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635862908390-1080x716.png 1080w" data-sizes="(max-width: 1206px) 100vw, 1206px"><p id="caption-attachment-672786" class="wp-caption-text">来源：在三年的驻村工作中磨练意志，锤炼党性，锻造灵魂 / 古道西风 （<a href="https://web.archive.org/web/20200918190431/https:/www.meipian.cn/295uiimr?first_share_uid=1000&amp;share_user_mpuuid=3956109775e7c895a139be693e48edb8&amp;share_depth=1&amp;first_share_to=other&amp;v=6.2.3&amp;user_id=1000&amp;share_from=others&amp;uuid=51a0173efffa4fe3a2d3616f1c9e3323&amp;isappinstalled=1&amp;idfa=B18B5F85-3D8F-4D08-8254-11137476313E">链接</a>）</p></div><p>克拉玛依市的一份官方文件显示，被拘留者从再教育营释放时的手续工作由当地人力资源和社会保障局负责处理。<span id="easy-footnote-341-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-341-672976" title="‘List of municipal government personnel and responsibilities, 2018’ [市级部门权责清单(2018年版]], Karamay District People’s Government [克拉玛依区人民政府], online. "><sup>&nbsp;[341]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>在南疆的鄯善县，被拘留者的食物和生活费用由司法局承担。<span id="easy-footnote-342-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-342-672976" title="‘Release of the 2017 public final accounts of Xinjiang Pichan County People’s Government Justice Bureau’ [2017 年度新疆鄯善县人民政府司法局部门决算公开], Xinjiang Pichan County People’s Government Justice Bureau [新疆鄯善县人民政府司法局], 2017, online. "><sup>&nbsp;[342]&nbsp;</sup></a></span></p><h4>“访惠聚”</h4><p>如本报告第三章所述，“访惠聚”是一项持续的政策，它将官员们（多为汉人，也有平民）下放到维吾尔人和其他少数民族家进行家访或居住，期间对这些家庭进行监视和思想灌输。<span id="easy-footnote-343-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-343-672976" title=" ‘China: Visiting officials occupy homes in Muslim region—”Becoming Family” campaign Intensifies repression in Xinjiang’, Human Rights Watch, 13 May 2018, online. "><sup>&nbsp;[343]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>“访惠聚”的中文全称是“访民情、惠民生、聚民心”。2014年2月，新疆党委宣布了首轮“访惠聚”活动，并计划在三年中派出20万名干部到基层的社区和村庄去。<span id="easy-footnote-344-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-344-672976" title="358   ‘Release of the 2017 final account of the Xinjiang Pichan County People’s Government Department of Justice’ [2017年度新疆鄯善县人民政府司法局部门决算公开], Xinjiang Piqan County People’s Government Department of Justice [新疆鄯善县人民政府], online. "><sup>&nbsp;[344]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>后来，“访惠聚”与一个名为“民族团结一家亲”的类似项目合并，<span id="easy-footnote-345-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-345-672976" title="‘Becoming Family’ is also known in Chinese as 结对认亲, but this report adopts the usage of ‘民族团结一家亲’ which seems more commonly used in official documents. "><sup>&nbsp;[345]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>截至本文撰写时，项目仍在继续。</p><div class="ar-caption">图35：新疆自治区副主席哈德尔别克·哈木扎在莎车县进行家访。</div><div id="attachment_672787" style="width: 510px" class="wp-caption aligncenter"><noscript><img aria-describedby="caption-attachment-672787" src="https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635862995294.png" alt="" width="500" class="size-full wp-image-672787" srcset="https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635862995294.png 1208w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635862995294-300x196.png 300w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635862995294-1024x668.png 1024w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635862995294-768x501.png 768w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635862995294-1080x705.png 1080w" sizes="(max-width: 1208px) 100vw, 1208px"></noscript><img aria-describedby="caption-attachment-672787" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns=%22http://www.w3.org/2000/svg%22%20viewBox=%220%200%20500%20333.33333333333%22%3E%3C/svg%3E" data-src="https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635862995294.png" alt="" width="500" class="lazyload size-full wp-image-672787" data-srcset="https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635862995294.png 1208w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635862995294-300x196.png 300w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635862995294-1024x668.png 1024w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635862995294-768x501.png 768w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635862995294-1080x705.png 1080w" data-sizes="(max-width: 1208px) 100vw, 1208px"><p id="caption-attachment-672787" class="wp-caption-text">来源：在三年的驻村工作中磨练意志，锤炼党性，锻造灵魂 / 古道西风 （<a href="https://web.archive.org/web/20200918190431/https:/www.meipian.cn/295uiimr?first_share_uid=1000&amp;share_user_mpuuid=3956109775e7c895a139be693e48edb8&amp;share_depth=1&amp;first_share_to=other&amp;v=6.2.3&amp;user_id=1000&amp;share_from=others&amp;uuid=51a0173efffa4fe3a2d3616f1c9e3323&amp;isappinstalled=1&amp;idfa=B18B5F85-3D8F-4D08-8254-11137476313E">链接</a>）</p></div><p>“访惠聚”项目由各级组织部下的访惠聚办公室负责领导和组织。<span id="easy-footnote-346-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-346-672976" title="‘Xinjiang Fanghuiju review: A major fundamental policy to promote long-lasting stable rule’ [新疆”访惠聚”述评：推进长治久安的重大治本之策], Xinjiang Daily [新疆日报], 13 January 2015, online.  / Shi Xin [石鑫], ‘Xinjiang: Must ceaselessly continue to deepen Fanghuiju village-based work’ [新疆：不断把‘访惠聚’驻村工作引向深入], Xinjiang Daily [新疆日报] via Central People’s Government [中国政府网], 3 December 2016, online; ‘Release of the 2019 final accounts of Shayar County People’s Procuratorate’ [沙雅县人民检察院 2019 年度部门决算公开说明], online. "><sup>&nbsp;[346]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>2015年，新疆组织部出版了几本“访惠聚”手册，告诉参与者如何处理可能遇到的问题。例如，当一个家庭拒绝官员进入其家中时该怎么办，或者如何与被拘留者的家人互动。<span id="easy-footnote-347-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-347-672976" title="‘“Hundred questions and hundred examples”: Cadre handbooks in the Fanghuiju campaign’, Xinjiang Documentation Project, University of British Columbia, online. "><sup>&nbsp;[347]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>除了短期内提高党国在新疆的能见度外，“访惠聚”项目的意图也在于通过重组基层的政治格局来巩固党在基层的长期控制。<span id="easy-footnote-348-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-348-672976" title="‘Fanghuiju work teams in Cherchen County help the village “two committees” with elections’ [且末县‘访惠聚’工作组助力村‘两委’换届], Weekend Stories [周末故事会], 24 June 2016, online; ‘Fanghuiju work teams assist in constructing Aksu Prefecture’s grassroots party organisation’ [‘访惠聚’工作助力阿克苏地区基层党组织建设], Xinjiang Daily [新疆日报] via Tianshan News [天山网], 22 October 2018, online."><sup>&nbsp;[348]&nbsp;</sup></a></span></p><p>截至2016年，新疆访惠聚办公室由组织部长马学军领导，<span id="easy-footnote-349-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-349-672976" title=" ‘Xinjiang: Must ceaselessly continue to deepen Fanghuiju village-based work’, Xinjiang Daily, 3 December 2016, online. "><sup>&nbsp;[349]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>成员包括统战部、宣传部、党校、妇联、新疆政法委等部门的官员。<span id="easy-footnote-350-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-350-672976" title="‘Issued by the Xinjiang Fanghuiju Office on 18 March 2016: Notice on changes to the structure and division of responsibilities of the Xinjiang Fanghuiju program leading small group’ [2016年3月18日自治区‘访惠聚’活动办公室印发：新民组发〔2016〕6号《关于调整自治区‘访惠聚’活动领导小组办公室内设机构职责分工的通知》], Kunlun News [昆仑网], 23 March 2016, online.<br />"><sup>&nbsp;[350]&nbsp;</sup></a></span></p><p>2016年10月陈全国上任后，新疆党委发起了“民族团结一家亲”倡议，<span id="easy-footnote-351-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-351-672976" title="‘1.1 million cadres and 1.6 million people from all different ethnic groups in Xinjiang “become families”’ [新疆110万名干部职工与160万户各族群众结对认亲], Xinhua Net [新华网], 4 July 2018, online. "><sup>&nbsp;[351]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>要求所有新疆的党员干部、政府官员和国有企业的管理人员融入维吾尔人或其他少数民族家庭的生活，成为他们虚构的“亲戚”。<span id="easy-footnote-352-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-352-672976" title="358   Dake Kang, Yanan Wang, ‘China’s Uighurs told to share beds, meals with party members’, The Associate Press, 1 December 2018, online; ‘Xinjiang launches “Becoming Family” Initiative mass mobilisation meeting, Chen Quanguo makes a speech’ [新疆召开‘民族团结一家亲’活动动员大会 陈全国讲话], Xinjiang Daily [新疆日报] via People’s Daily Online [人民网], 17 October 2016, online; ‘Our “relatives” have arrived! &amp;#8211; True stories from the implementation of the “Becoming Family” Initiative in Xinjiang’ [我家‘亲戚’来了—新疆开展‘民族团结一家亲’活动纪实], Guangming Daily [光明日报] via Xinhua Net [新华网], 18 April 2020, online; ‘Endless heartwarming stories of mutual assistance among ethnicities from the Becoming Family Initiative in Xinjiang’ [新疆各族人民‘结亲’互助,暖心故事一千零一夜也讲不完], CCTV [央视网], 7 July 2018, online. "><sup>&nbsp;[352]&nbsp;</sup></a></span></p><div class="ar-caption">图36：陈全国在一次“民族团结一家亲”活动动员大会上讲话。</div><div id="attachment_672788" style="width: 510px" class="wp-caption aligncenter"><noscript><img href="https://freewechat.com/a/MzA5MDc1NDA1Mg==/2651369833/1">链接</a>）</p></div><p>2017年12月，新疆党委启动了第二轮“民族团结一家亲”活动，派出超过112万名干部和平民进入原住民家庭，每两个月居住五天。<span id="easy-footnote-353-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-353-672976" title="‘”Becoming Family” and helping each other, a new page in the history book of Xinjiang’s ethnic unity’<br />[结对认亲,守望相助!两年了,新疆民族团结史册翻开崭新一页!], Xinjiang United Front Work Department [新疆维统一战线], 3 January 2019, online. "><sup>&nbsp;[353]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>从日常工作上来看，“民族团结一家亲”活动是“访惠聚”的延伸，并与“访惠聚”合并，<span id="easy-footnote-354-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-354-672976" title="Chang Chenxuan [张晨暄], ‘The Becoming Family Initiative will deepen the progress of Fanghuiju work’ [‘民族团结一家亲’活动将“访惠聚”工作推向深入], Yaxin News [亚心网] via Phoenix News [凤凰新闻], 20 October 2016, online; ‘All levels of Fanghuiju village-based work teams actively participate in the Becoming Family Initiative in Bayingolin Prefecture’ [巴州各‘访惠聚’驻村工作队积极开展‘民族团结一家亲’活动], Sohu News [搜狐新闻], 27 August 2018, online; ‘Cadres go to grassroots and synergize “Becoming Family” with Fanghuiju campaign’ [【民族团结】干部俯下身子下基层,把‘民族团结一家亲’与‘访惠聚’相互贯穿], Prefecture CPPCC Guangming Neighbourhood work team on WeChat [州政协驻光明社区工作队微信公众号”尉犁零距离”], 11 May 2019, online."><sup>&nbsp;[354]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>尽管“民族团结一家亲”领导小组和办公室隶属于统战部，而非组织部。<span id="easy-footnote-355-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-355-672976" title="‘Toli County tours conference to highlight positive Becoming Family Initiative examples’ [托里县开展‘民族团结一家 亲’先进典型事迹巡回报告会], ‘Becoming Family’ Initiative Leading Small Group on WeChat “[   民族团结一家亲”活动 领导小组微信公众号”托里零距离”] via Sohu News [搜狐新闻], 4 July 2019, online; ‘The County’s United Front Work Department arranges batches of training for cadres on ethnic unity &amp;#8211; to strengthen their theories and improve their overall capabilities’ [民族团结一家亲]强化理论培训提升综合素质 —县委统战部分批次举办民族团结工作分管领导培训], Ürümqi County Zero Distance [乌鲁木齐县零距离], 28 January 2019, online; ‘Hejing County holds meeting on “Becoming Family” Initiative Advancement’ [和静县召开‘民族团结一家亲’活动推进会], Hejing Zero Distance [和静零距离], 24 September 2017, online; ‘Window into the leadership team’ [领导之窗], Xinjiang United Front Work Department [新疆统一战线], online. "><sup>&nbsp;[355]&nbsp;</sup></a></span></p><p>自2017年以来，管理自治区访惠聚办公室的“自治区访惠聚领导小组”由陈全国亲自领导。<span id="easy-footnote-356-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-356-672976" title="‘Fanghuiju work winning praises’ [‘访惠聚’工作赢赞誉], Kargilik County People’s Government [叶城县人民政府], 6 July 2017, online. "><sup>&nbsp;[356]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>同年，新疆发展和改革委员会开发了一套信息管理系统，以提高“访惠聚”的效率。<span id="easy-footnote-357-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-357-672976" title="‘Xinjiang Information Centre’ [新疆自治区信息中心], TSP Web [调色盘网], 15 January 2021, online. "><sup>&nbsp;[357]&nbsp;</sup></a></span></p><p>新疆几乎每个部门和办公室都会派干部参加“访惠聚”项目，包括那些通常与监视或民族政策无关的部门，如住房和城乡建设厅<span id="easy-footnote-358-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-358-672976" title="‘Villager Helpitim Imin organised marriage for his daughters twice, and the two experiences were radically different’ [村民海皮提木·依明两次嫁女儿前后大不同], Xinjiang Department of Housing and Urban–Rural Development<br />[新疆维吾尔自治区住房和城乡建设厅], 6 April 2016, online. "><sup>&nbsp;[358]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>以及农牧业机械管理局。<span id="easy-footnote-359-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-359-672976" title="‘Xinjiang further implements the Fanghuiju Program: Questions and answers for those who conduct village-based work’ [自治区深化‘访民情惠民生聚民心’:驻村工作应知应会问答], Xinjiang Agricultural Machinery Bureau<br />[新疆维吾尔自治区农牧业机械管理局], 12 March 2018, online. "><sup>&nbsp;[359]&nbsp;</sup></a></span></p><h4>强迫劳动</h4><p>在再教育运动期间，来自南疆农村地区的维吾尔人和其他少数民族被称为“富余劳动力”或“贫困劳动力”，并被送往新疆其他地区或其他省份的工厂工作。<span id="easy-footnote-360-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-360-672976" title="‘Three years of education and aid have inspired southern Xinjiang ‘surplus labourers’ to be motivated to rise out of poverty’ [三年教育帮扶，激发南疆富余劳动力脱贫‘心’动力], China Xinjiang News [中国新疆网], 2 April 2020, online; Aynur [阿依努尔], ‘Southern Xinjiang implements “surplus labour” transfer and employment with precision’ [新疆精准推进南疆富余劳动力转移就业], Bingtuan Daily [兵团日报], 13 October 2019, online; Adrian Zenz, ‘Coercive labor and forced displacement in Xinjiang’s cross-regional labor transfer program’, Jamestown Foundation, March 2021, online."><sup>&nbsp;[360]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>据国家媒体报道，当局打算在2017年至2021年期间培训60万名来自南疆的“富余劳动力”，并把他们转移到其他地方去工作。<span id="easy-footnote-361-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-361-672976" title="Li Fangfang [李芳芳], ‘Story from southern Xinjiang: labour transfer within Xinjiang helps removing the label of poverty’ [南疆故事:疆内转移就业,摘掉贫穷标签], Beijing Review [北京周报], 15 December 2017, online. "><sup>&nbsp;[361]&nbsp;</sup></a></span></p><p>ASPI之前的报告《待售的维吾尔人》 （Uyghurs for sale）指出，在远离家乡的工厂里，维吾尔工人通常和其他工人分开住，并在工作时间之外接受有组织的汉语和意识形态培训。他们受到持续监视，宗教信仰被禁止。<span id="easy-footnote-362-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-362-672976" title="Xu et al., Uyghurs for sale. "><sup>&nbsp;[362]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>中国媒体2017年报道说，在党的干部到偏远的皮山县的各家各户施压以前，没有一位村民自愿报名加入劳动力转移计划、前往4000公里外的安徽省工作。<span id="easy-footnote-363-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-363-672976" title="John Sudworth, ‘“If the others go I’ll go”: Inside China’s scheme to transfer Uighurs into work’, BBC News, 2 March 2020, online. "><sup>&nbsp;[363]&nbsp;</sup></a></span></p><p>新疆自治区人力资源和社会保障厅直接负责这些大规模的工作分配。该部门为“贫困劳动力”提供“免费培训”，<span id="easy-footnote-364-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-364-672976" title="‘Xinjiang trains all of southern Xinjiang’s “poverty-stricken labourers”’’ [新疆维吾尔自治区全员培训南疆贫困劳动力], Ministry of Human Resources and Social Security [中国人力资源和社会保障部], 9 February 2019, online."><sup>&nbsp;[364]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>并为参与企业提供补贴。<span id="easy-footnote-365-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-365-672976" title="‘Xinjiang Department of Human Resources and Social Security: Strengthen cooperation on labour administration within Xinjiang and further long-term stable employment’ [新疆自治区人力资源和社会保障厅：强化区内劳务协作,促进长期稳定就业], Ministry of Human Resources and Social Stability [中国人力资源和社会保障部], 11 January 2019, online; Zhang Qiongwen [张琼文], ‘Organising across regions, matching needs with skills &amp;#8211; 50,000 from Xinjiang have been systematically transferred and assumed employment’ [跨区域组织,精准化对接——新疆5万名跨区域有组织转移人员稳岗就业], National Administration for Rural Revitalisation [国家乡村振兴局], 31 July 2020, online."><sup>&nbsp;[365]&nbsp;</sup></a></span></p><p>2018年底，自治区成立“南疆四地州深度贫困地区有组织转移就业工作领导小组”，负责劳动力转移工作，由自治区组织部长领导。<span id="easy-footnote-366-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-366-672976" title="‘Xinjiang Department of Human Resources and Social Security: Must strengthen cooperation within labour<br />administration in Xinjiang and further long-term employment stability among its people’, 11 January 2019, online; ‘Six batches of labour transfer help 100,000 people to escape poverty’’ [‘六个一批’转移就业助十万群众摆脱贫困], China Public Jobs Announcement Online [中国公共招聘网], 28 December 2018, online. "><sup>&nbsp;[366]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>该小组的地方分支机构通常由各地党政领导牵头，由当地人力资源和社会保障局协调。<span id="easy-footnote-367-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-367-672976" title="‘Nilqa County, Xinjiang: Many measures combined to explore and improve new models to transfer rural labourers outside Xinjiang’ [新疆尼勒克：多措并举探索提升农村劳动力疆外有组织转移就业新模式], China’s Employment Online [中国就业网], 24 June 2019, online; Guang Xiangli [关祥利], ‘Orku District, Karamay City, Xinjiang: Arrange southern Xinjiang’s transferred labourers to settle down, in order to win the final battle against persistent poverty’ [新疆克拉玛依市乌尔禾区：妥善安置南疆富余劳动力,助力决战决胜脱贫攻坚], People’s Daily Online [人民网], 30 March 2020, online. "><sup>&nbsp;[367]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>2017年，哈密市伊州区的一份政府文件指出，该地劳动力转移工作小组向其成员部门分配转移名额。<span id="easy-footnote-368-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-368-672976" title="‘2017 implementation plan for Iwirghol district, Qumul city to systematically transfer rural “surplus labourers” for employment’ [2017年新疆哈密市伊州区农村富余劳动力有组织转移就业实施方案], Qumul City Iwirghol District People’s Government [哈密市伊州区人民政府], 30 October 2017, online."><sup>&nbsp;[368]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>另一份政府新闻稿称，尼勒克县的每位官员都被分配了转移名额。<span id="easy-footnote-369-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-369-672976" title="‘Nilqa County, Xinjiang: Need to explore new models of organised labour transfer of surplus rural labour’,<br />China’s Employment Online, 24 June 2019, online. "><sup>&nbsp;[369]&nbsp;</sup></a></span></p><p>多份各级政府文件表明，转移就业人员有人负责看守，行动自由受限。<span id="easy-footnote-370-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-370-672976" title="Xu et al., Uyghurs for sale. "><sup>&nbsp;[370]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>新疆人力资源和社会保障厅雇用双语看守来监督少数民族工人，并运行一个名为“农村劳动力转移就业管理系统”的监控体系，实时追踪工人。<span id="easy-footnote-371-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-371-672976" title="‘Xinjiang Department of Human Resources and Social Security: Must strengthen cooperation within labour administration in Xinjiang and further long-term employment stability among its people’, 11 January 2019, online; ‘Organising across regions, matching needs with skills &amp;#8211; 50,000 from Xinjiang have been systematically transferred and assumed employment’ National Administration for Rural Revitalisation, 31 July 2020, online; ‘Labour transfer leads to better lives’ [转移就业:让日子越来越美好], Xinjiang Daily [新疆日报], 10 August 2019, online. "><sup>&nbsp;[371]&nbsp;</sup></a></span></p><p>焉耆回族自治县的一份政府文件显示，未经县级和地市级劳动力转移工作领导小组批准，转移来的工人不得离开工作岗位或回家。<span id="easy-footnote-372-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-372-672976" title="‘Notice on the further improvement of the employment stability of the organised transfer labour force in deeply impoverished areas of the four Southern Xinjiang prefectures’ [关于进一步提高南疆四地州深度贫困地区有组织转移劳动力就业稳定性工作的通知], Office of the Karashahar Hui Autonomous County People’s Government [焉耆回族自治县人民政府办公室], 20 November 2018, online. "><sup>&nbsp;[372]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>任何与工人行为有关的“异常情况”都会被报备给县级政法委、公安局和劳动力转移工作领导小组。<span id="easy-footnote-373-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-373-672976" title="‘Notice on the further improvement of the employment stability of the organised transfer labour force in deeply impoverished areas of the four Southern Xinjiang prefectures’ [关于进一步提高南疆四地州深度贫困地区有组织转移劳动力就业稳定性工作的通知], Office of the Karashahar Hui Autonomous County People’s Government [焉耆回族自治县人民政府办公室], 20 November 2018, online. "><sup>&nbsp;[373]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>《华盛顿邮报》记者2020年访问青岛的一家耐克代工厂时，也发现维吾尔工人不被允许回家，并且工厂的外观好似一座监狱。<span id="easy-footnote-374-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-374-672976" title="Anna Fifield, ‘China compels Uighurs to work in shoe factory that supplies Nike’, Washington Post, 29 February 2020, online. "><sup>&nbsp;[374]&nbsp;</sup></a></span></p><div class="ar-caption">图37：维吾尔工人梅合热阿依·吐合提和同工厂的所有其他工人一样，手写承诺书“发声亮剑”。</div><div id="attachment_672789" style="width: 510px" class="wp-caption aligncenter"><noscript><img aria-describedby="caption-attachment-672789" src="https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635863199152.png" alt="" width="500" class="size-full https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635863199152-1024x592.png 1024w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635863199152-768x444.png 768w, src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns=%22http://www.w3.org/2000/svg%22%20viewBox=%220%200%20500%20333.33333333333%22%3E%3C/svg%3E"
