data-srcset="https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635863199152.png 1146w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635863199152-300x173.png 300w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635863199152-1024x592.png 1024w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635863199152-768x444.png 768w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635863199152-1080x624.png 1080w" data-sizes="(max-width: 1146px) 100vw, 1146px"><p id="caption-attachment-672789" class="wp-caption-text">民族团结 | 持续发声亮剑 誓与“三股势力”作斗争 / 今日圣雄（微信公众号）2018年5月18日（<a href="https://archive.ph/K2yNY%2523selection-49.25-50.0">链接</a>）<br></p></div><p>作为劳动力转移计划的一部分，新疆内外的多个部门被要求负责为维吾尔人和其他少数民族在特定行业“落实岗位”。<span id="easy-footnote-375-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-375-672976" title=" ‘The 2017 plan to implement organised transfer of surplus labour for the purpose of poverty alleviation in Iwirghol District, Qumul city, Xinjiang’ [2017年新疆哈密市伊州区农村富余劳动力有组织转移就业实施方案], Qumul City Iwirghol District People’s Government [哈密市伊州区人民政府], 30 October 2017, online; ‘Xinjiang Department of Human Resources and Social Security: Must strengthen cooperation within labour administration in Xinjiang and<br />further long-term employment stability among its people’, Ministry of Human Resources and Social Stability, 11 January 2019, online. "><sup>&nbsp;[375]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>这些“创造就业”的行为并非提供福利，而是迫使维吾尔人和其他原住民离开他们的家园，打散社区和家庭。<span id="easy-footnote-376-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-376-672976" title="Zenz, Coercive labor and forced displacement in Xinjiang’s cross-regional labor transfer program. "><sup>&nbsp;[376]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>被转移的工人通常在18岁至40岁之间，<span id="easy-footnote-377-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-377-672976" title="‘Nilqa County, Xinjiang: Need to explore new models of organised labour transfer of surplus rural labour’ [新疆尼勒 克：多措并举探索提升农村劳动力疆外有组织转移就业新模式], China’s Employment Online [中国就业网], 24 June 2019, online; ‘The 2017 plan to implement organised transfer of surplus labour for the purpose of poverty alleviation in Iwirghol district, Qumul city, Xinjiang’, Qumul City Iwirghol District People’s Government, 30 October 2017, online. "><sup>&nbsp;[377]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>其中许多人留下了孩子、老人和牲畜。<span id="easy-footnote-378-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-378-672976" title="‘Organising across regions, matching needs with skills &amp;#8211; 50,000 from Xinjiang have been systematically transferred and assumed employment’ National Administration for Rural Revitalisation, 31 July 2020, online. "><sup>&nbsp;[378]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>例如，在实施劳动力转移计划后，叶城县（维吾尔人占93%<span id="easy-footnote-379-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-379-672976" title="‘About the People’s Court of Kargilik County, Kashgar Prefecture, Xinjiang’ [新疆喀什地区叶城县人民法院], Xinjiang Judicial Litigation Service [新疆法院诉讼服务网], online. "><sup>&nbsp;[379]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>）有2428名老年居民、1941名儿童和约33.69万头牲畜被留给国家照顾。<span id="easy-footnote-380-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-380-672976" title="‘Organising across regions, matching needs with skills &amp;#8211; 50,000 from Xinjiang have been systematically transferred and assumed employment’, National Administration for Rural Revitalisation, 31 July 2020, online. "><sup>&nbsp;[380]&nbsp;</sup></a></span></p><p>新疆发改委将工人转移到固定资产投资项目，这些项目包括基础设施建设和其他国有项目。<span id="easy-footnote-381-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-381-672976" title=" ‘Notice on the further improvement of the employment stability of the organised labour transfers in deeply<br />poverty-stricken areas of the four southern Xinjiang prefectures’ [关于进一步提高南疆四地州深度贫困地区有组织转移劳动力就业稳定性工作的通知], Office of the Karashahar Hui Autonomous County People’s Government [焉耆回族自治县人民政府办公室], 20 November 2018, online; ‘Investment in fixed assets from January to February 2020’, National Bureau of Statistics of China, 17 March 2020, online. "><sup>&nbsp;[381]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>2017年至2019年期间，自治区国有资产监督管理委员会将1.6万名“贫困劳动力”向国有企业转移。<span id="easy-footnote-382-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-382-672976" title="Commonly known in English by its acronym SASAC. / ‘Xinjiang’s district-level state-owned enterprises and central-government-level state-owned enterprises absorb nearly a thousand labourers from poor families in deeply poverty-stricken counties in southern Xinjiang’s four prefectures’ [自治区区属国企及中央驻疆企业吸纳首批近千名,南疆四地州深度贫困县贫困家庭劳动力就业], Xinjiang Kunlun News [新疆昆仑网], 31 March 2020, online. "><sup>&nbsp;[382]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>人力资源和社会保障部将工人转移到公益性岗位。自治区工业和信息化厅将工人转移到纺织、服装、农业和电子制造业。<span id="easy-footnote-383-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-383-672976" title="390   ‘Government Information Release: Nijat Ismayil’ [政府信息公开: 尼加提•司马义], Xinjiang Industry and Information Technology Department [新疆维吾尔自治区工业和信息化厅], December 2020, online; Li Chunxia, ‘Labour transfer leads to better lives’, Xinjiang Daily, 10 August 2019, online; ‘Prefecture Industry and Information Technology Bureau personnel and responsibilities’ [地区工业和信息化局班子成员分工], Xinjiang Altay Prefecture Administration [新疆阿勒泰地区行署], 26 May 2019, online; ‘Kizilsu Prefecture Industry and Information Technology Bureau information release &amp;#8211; Leadership personnel list’ [克州工业和信息化局信息公开-领导成员], Xinjiang Kizilsu Kyrgyz Autonomous Prefecture People’s Government [新疆维吾尔自治区克州人民政府], online; ‘7th national Xinjiang Aid work conference met with enthusiastic responses in Xinjiang’ [第七次全国对口支援新疆工作会议在新疆维吾尔自治区引发热烈反响], Xinjiang Daily [新疆日报] via People’s Daily Online [人民网], 18 July 2019, online; Amy K Lehr, ‘Addressing forced labor in the Xinjiang Uyghur Autonomous Region: Toward a shared agenda’, Center for Strategic and International Studies, 30 July 2020, online. ‘Record of the Prefecture’s Xinjiang Aid efforts (2) Industrial Xinjiang Aid to promote development and help benefit people’s livelihood’ [州援疆风采录（2）产业援疆促发展增添动力惠民生], Changji Daily on WeChat [《昌吉日报》微信公众号”昌吉市零距离”], 31 December 2019, online. "><sup>&nbsp;[383]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>住房和城乡建设厅将工人转移到建筑行业。<span id="easy-footnote-384-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-384-672976" title="390   Gong Houyu [龚后雨], Wang Ganggang [王刚刚], ‘Xinjiang Department of Housing and Urban-Rural Development: Provide housing for all farmers and herdsmen from all ethnicities’ [新疆维吾尔自治区住房和城乡建设厅村镇建设处： 让各族农牧民住有安居], National Administration for Rural Revitalisation [国家乡村振兴局], 25 February 2021, online; ‘“Years as long as rivers, waves as loud as songs”: Recollections of Quan He, Deputy Director of Xinjiang’s Department of Housing and Urban-Rural Development’ [岁月如河 澎湃如歌——记新疆住房和城乡建设厅副厅长全河], China Construction News [中国建设报], 20 September 2019, online. "><sup>&nbsp;[384]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>自治区扶贫开发办公室与中华全国工商业联合会协调，将民营企业引入南疆，为转移就业做准备。<span id="easy-footnote-385-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-385-672976" title="‘Speech by Liu Yongfu at the 2019 tour of private enterprises in southern Xinjiang’ [在2019‘民营企业南疆行’活动上的讲话-刘永富], National Administration for Rural Revitalisation [国家乡村振兴局], 25 February 2020, online. "><sup>&nbsp;[385]&nbsp;</sup></a></span></p><div class="ar-caption">图38：在托克逊县一座工厂，从南疆来的转移劳动力在进行“发声亮剑”仪式。</div><div id="attachment_672790" style="width: 510px" class="wp-caption aligncenter"><noscript><img aria-describedby="caption-attachment-672790" src="https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635863296877.png" alt="" width="500" class="size-full wp-image-672790" srcset="https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635863296877.png 1196w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635863296877-300x198.png 300w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635863296877-1024x676.png 1024w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635863296877-768x507.png 768w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635863296877-1080x713.png 1080w" sizes="(max-width: 1196px) 100vw, 1196px"></noscript><img aria-describedby="caption-attachment-672790" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns=%22http://www.w3.org/2000/svg%22%20viewBox=%220%200%20500%20333.33333333333%22%3E%3C/svg%3E" data-src="https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635863296877.png" alt="" width="500" class="lazyload size-full wp-image-672790" data-srcset="https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635863296877.png 1196w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635863296877-300x198.png 300w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635863296877-1024x676.png 1024w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635863296877-768x507.png 768w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635863296877-1080x713.png 1080w" data-sizes="(max-width: 1196px) 100vw, 1196px"><p id="caption-attachment-672790" class="wp-caption-text">民族团结 | 持续发声亮剑 誓与“三股势力”作斗争 / 今日圣雄（微信公众号）2018年5月18日（<a href="https://archive.ph/K2yNY%2523selection-49.25-50.0">链接</a>）<br></p></div><p>其他理论上劳务无关的党政机关也参与了劳动力转移。例如在2019年，于田县妇联将50名妇女送到山东青岛的一家电子厂工作，另将500名妇女送到乌鲁木齐从事家政和餐饮服务工作。<span id="easy-footnote-386-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-386-672976" title="‘Keriye County promotes women’s labour transfer and employment’ [于田县推进妇女劳务输出转移就业工作],<br />Keriye County Government Net [于田政府网], 25 January 2019, online."><sup>&nbsp;[386]&nbsp;</sup></a></span></p><p>“访惠聚”工作队还走访了一些家庭，并进行了“调查”（具体调查内容未写明），试图说服维吾尔人和其他少数民族接受被分配的工作。<span id="easy-footnote-387-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-387-672976" title="Duan Yuqiang [段玉强], ‘Work team assists the first groups of rural surplus labourers from Baghchi village with labour transfer’ [工作队帮助巴格其村首批农村富余劳动力转移就业], Legal Culture Medias [法制文化传媒], 9 March 2018, online."><sup>&nbsp;[387]&nbsp;</sup></a></span></p><h4>人口控制</h4><p>在再教育运动期间，新疆当局对“违法生育”进行了一系列的打击，以压低维吾尔和其他少数民族妇女的生育率。<span id="easy-footnote-388-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-388-672976" title="Ruser &amp;amp; Leibold, Family de-planning: the coercive campaign to drive down indigenous birth-rates in Xinjiang; ‘China cuts Uighur births with IUDs, abortion, sterilization’, The Associated Press, 29 June 2020, online; Adrian Zenz, Sterilizations, IUDs, and mandatory birth control: the CCP’s campaign to suppress Uyghur birthrates in Xinjiang, Jamestown Foundation, June 2020, online. "><sup>&nbsp;[388]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>违反“计划生育”政策的少数民族妇女，一经发现则面临高额罚款、纪律处分、拘留和强制绝育等。<span id="easy-footnote-389-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-389-672976" title="Ibid. "><sup>&nbsp;[389]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>甚至早在1992年发生的“违法生育”都受到追溯性地惩罚。<span id="easy-footnote-390-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-390-672976" title=" ‘Notice on launching retrospective targeted crackdown against illegal births’ [关于开展违法生育专项治理“回头看”工作的通知], Ulughchat County People’s Government [乌恰县人民政府], 16 June 2018, online; ‘Gumudi Township’s plans on “two types of thorough investigations” during targeted campaign against illegal births’ [关于印发《古牧地镇2019年违法生育‘两个彻查’专项行动实施方案》的通知], Midong District People’s Government [米东区人民政府], 21 July 2019, online."><sup>&nbsp;[390]&nbsp;</sup></a></span></p><p>因此，在2017年到2019年的两年间，新疆政府公布的生育率下降了近一半（48.74%）。<span id="easy-footnote-391-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-391-672976" title="Ruser &amp;amp; Leibold, Family de-planning: the coercive campaign to drive down indigenous birth-rates in Xinjiang."><sup>&nbsp;[391]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>在原住民比例较高的南疆，生育率下降幅度更加剧烈。<span id="easy-footnote-392-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-392-672976" title="Ibid. "><sup>&nbsp;[392]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>这些“计划生育”措施专门针对维吾尔人和其他原住民群体，而在中国其他地区，中共党国为了提高出生率，正在试图阻碍汉人妇女进行非医疗必须的堕胎。<span id="easy-footnote-393-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-393-672976" title="Kaamil Ahmed, ‘China to clamp down on abortions for “non-medical purposes”’, The Guardian, 28 September 2021, online; Sui-Lee Wee, ‘China says it will allow couples to have 3 children, up from 2’, The New York Times, 31 May 2021, online; Nathan Vanderklippe, ‘How China is trying to limit births among Muslim populations in Xinjiang region’, The Globe and Mail, 24 June 2021, online."><sup>&nbsp;[393]&nbsp;</sup></a></span></p><div class="ar-caption">图39：1991年至2019年新疆与全国粗出生率对比</div><div id="attachment_672791" style="width: 510px" class="wp-caption aligncenter"><noscript><img aria-describedby="caption-attachment-672791" src="https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635863369749.png" alt="" width="500" class="size-full wp-image-672791" srcset="https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635863369749.png 944w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635863369749-300x153.png 300w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635863369749-768x391.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 944px) 100vw, 944px"></noscript><img aria-describedby="caption-attachment-672791" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns=%22http://www.w3.org/2000/svg%22%20viewBox=%220%200%20500%20333.33333333333%22%3E%3C/svg%3E" data-src="https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635863369749.png" alt="" width="500" class="lazyload size-full wp-image-672791" data-srcset="https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635863369749.png 944w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635863369749-300x153.png 300w, https://chinadigitaltimes.net/chinese/files/2021/11/image-1635863369749-768x391.png 768w" data-sizes="(max-width: 944px) 100vw, 944px"><p id="caption-attachment-672791" class="wp-caption-text">来源：内森·鲁瑟、雷国俊《新疆计划生育报告》 / ASPI 2021年5月12日（<a href="https://www.aspi.org.au/report/family-deplanning-birthrates-xinjiang">链接</a>）<br></p></div><p>一份泄露出来的墨玉县拘留名单显示，<span id="easy-footnote-394-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-394-672976" title="‘Population data of Karakash County’ [墨玉县人口数据], Red Black Population Statistics Library [红黑人口库], 20 July 2020, online. "><sup>&nbsp;[394]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>484名被拘留者中有149人是因为子女过多而被拘留的。<span id="easy-footnote-395-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-395-672976" title="‘China cuts Uighur births with IUDs, abortion, sterilization’, The Associated Press, 29 June 2020, online. "><sup>&nbsp;[395]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>2017年，维族水果商人阿卜杜舒库尔·尤玛（Abdushukur Umar）被关进再教育营，后来被判处有期徒刑七年。他的亲属在接受美联社采访时说，当局告诉他们尤玛有七个孩子，每个孩子多判一年，所以被判了七年刑。<span id="easy-footnote-396-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-396-672976" title="Ibid. "><sup>&nbsp;[396]&nbsp;</sup></a></span></p><p>新疆计划生育政策主要由新疆卫健委负责。仅在2020年一年，新疆卫健委就花费1.4亿人民币（合2200万美元）用于降低出生率和打击南疆的“违法生育”。<span id="easy-footnote-397-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-397-672976" title="‘Release of the 2020 departmental budget of the Xinjiang Health Commission’ [新疆维吾尔自治区卫生健康委员会2020年度部门预算公开报告], online. "><sup>&nbsp;[397]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>继2017年和2018年新疆卫健委出台计划生育工作指示后，<span id="easy-footnote-398-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-398-672976" title="‘Notice on the launch of Koktogay County’s target campaign against illegal births’ [关于印发《富蕴县开展违法生育专项治理行动实施方案》的通知], Koktogay County People’s Government [富蕴县人民政府], 30 April 2019, online; ‘Notice on Cherchen County’s 2018 targeted crackdown against illegal births’ [关于印发《且末县2018年度违法生育专项治理工作实施方案》的通知], Cherchen County People’s Government [且末县人民政府], 30 May 2018, online. "><sup>&nbsp;[398]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>新疆各地区、<span id="easy-footnote-399-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-399-672976" title="‘Population management leading small group convenes on video conference’ [统筹解决人口问题领导小组视频会召开], Xinjiang People’s Government [新疆人民政府], 23 November 2018, online; ‘Notice on the establishment of the prefecture’s illegal births crackdown leading small group’ [关于成立自治州违法生育治理工作领导小组的通知], Law-Lib [法律图书馆], 21 August 2017, online. "><sup>&nbsp;[399]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>县、<span id="easy-footnote-400-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-400-672976" title="‘Release of plans on Koktogay County’s targeted crackdown against illegal births‘, Koktogay County People’s Government, 30 April 2019, online. "><sup>&nbsp;[400]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>乡以及政府部门和公司内部都成立了“违法生育专项治理行动领导小组”。<span id="easy-footnote-401-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-401-672976" title="‘Notice on Cherchen County’s 2018 targeted crackdown against illegal births’, Cherchen County People’s Government, 30 May 2018, online."><sup>&nbsp;[401]&nbsp;</sup></a></span></p><p>该领导小组的办公室设在卫健委内，其成员包括来自各种党政机关的官员，如公安局、统战部、宣传部、教育部、妇联、纪律检查委员会、民族宗教事务局、民政局、财政局、人力资源和社会保障局、司法局等。<span id="easy-footnote-402-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-402-672976" title="‘Notice on Cherchen County’s 2018 targeted crackdown against illegal births’, Cherchen County People’s Government, 30 May 2018, online; ‘Release of plans on Koktogay County’s targeted crackdown against illegal births‘, Koktogay County People’s Government, 30 April 2019, online. "><sup>&nbsp;[402]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>于2017年修订的《新疆维吾尔自治区人口与计划生育条例》也将上述大部分机构列为帮助实施计划生育政策的部门。<span id="easy-footnote-403-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-403-672976" title="‘Xinjiang Regulation on Population and Family Planning’ [新疆维吾尔自治区人口与计划生育条例], Xinjiang Health Commission [新疆维吾尔自治区卫生健康委员会], 17 July 2019, online. "><sup>&nbsp;[403]&nbsp;</sup></a></span></p><p>在基层，居/村委会书记、“访惠聚”工作队、计生工作人员和网格员负责对实施与违法生育整治行动相关的日常工作。<span id="easy-footnote-404-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-404-672976" title=" ‘Qaradong Township launches the 2017 conference on targeted crackdown against illegal births’ [喀尔墩乡召开2017年违法生育专项治理工作会议], Qaradong Township People’s Government [喀尔墩乡人民政府], 8 April 2017, online."><sup>&nbsp;[404]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>惩治违法生育是地方官员的一项重要业绩指标，<span id="easy-footnote-405-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-405-672976" title="‘Notice on launching retrospective targeted crackdown against illegal births’ [关于开展违法生育专项治理“回头看”工作的通知], Ulughchat County People’s Government [乌恰县人民政府], 16 June 2018, online."><sup>&nbsp;[405]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>而官员们本人如果一旦被发现违反计划生育规定，就可能立即被降职或解职。<span id="easy-footnote-406-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-406-672976" title="‘Notice on continuing and advancing targeted crackdown against illegal births’ [关于持续深入开展违法生育专项治理工作的通知], Qapqal Xibe Autonomous County People’s Government [察布查尔县人民政府], 28 May 2018, online."><sup>&nbsp;[406]&nbsp;</sup></a></span></p><p>在减少维吾尔和其他少数民族生育的行动开始之前，习近平曾在2014年指示新疆生产建设兵团<span id="easy-footnote-407-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-407-672976" title="A Han-majority paramilitary organisation acting like a state within a state in Xinjiang. "><sup>&nbsp;[407]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>“优化人口资源”。<span id="easy-footnote-408-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-408-672976" title="‘Using industries to attract people: Develop industries in order to create jobs and gather more population’ [以产引人： 发展产业带动就业集聚人口], Bingtuan Daily [兵团日报], 25 April 2019, online. "><sup>&nbsp;[408]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>兵团是以汉人为主的准军事组织，它将该指令理解为优先人口扩张，特别是在维吾尔人为主的南疆。<span id="easy-footnote-409-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-409-672976" title="Ibid. "><sup>&nbsp;[409]&nbsp;</sup></a></span></p><h2>第八章：结论</h2><p>本文通过研究中共党国的治理方法，阐明了新疆的人权侵犯是如何进行、由谁来执行的。以实现政治调整为目的而进行的大规模运动并非是旧时代的产物，相反，它们正发生在中国社会与世界的联系比以往任何时候都更加紧密的、当下的时代。而且，新疆的运动沿着种族和宗教两条线展开，产生了十分深刻的社会影响。这也是众多民主国家第一次近距离经历中国的大规模运动，同时有意或无意地消费其产出，如强迫劳动的产品。<span id="easy-footnote-410-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-410-672976" title="Xu et al., Uyghurs for sale."><sup>&nbsp;[410]&nbsp;</sup></a></span></p><p>新疆官僚机构的内部运作和中国更大范围的威权统治模式是局部与整体的关系。事实上，新疆两次运动期间使用的许多治理手段是在其他地方构思出来的，如2004年北京率先启用的网格化管理制度，<span id="easy-footnote-411-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-411-672976" title="Wu Qiang, ‘Urban grid management and police state in China: a brief overview’, China Change, 12 August 2014, online. "><sup>&nbsp;[411]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>以及2015年在西藏先行的十户联防制度。<span id="easy-footnote-412-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-412-672976" title="‘1,202 “advanced joint households” families are commended in Tibet, as more than 3,000 representatives of joint households are elected to the village “two committees”’ [西藏表彰1202户‘先进双联户’家庭 3000多名联户代表选进村‘两委’], China Peace [长安网], 6 January 2015, online. "><sup>&nbsp;[412]&nbsp;</sup></a></span></p><p>新疆的一些治理手段也在其他地方得到了推广。2017年，新疆政法委接待了来自中央政府和其他省份的22个考察团。<span id="easy-footnote-413-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-413-672976" title="‘Release of the 2017 Xinjiang PLAC’s final departmental accounts’ [2017年度自治区党委政法委部门决算公开说明], Xinjiang People’s Government [新疆维吾尔自治区人民政府], 31 August 2017, online. "><sup>&nbsp;[413]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>2018年，宁夏政法委书记张韵声在视察了新疆的维稳指挥部和一体化联合作战平台后，表示要“学习借鉴”新疆的经验。<span id="easy-footnote-414-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-414-672976" title="Deng Zhihua [邓志华], ‘Ningxia PLAC and other departments went to Xinjiang to inspect and dock counterterrorism and stability maintenance work’ [宁夏党委政法委等部门赴新疆考察对接反恐维稳工作], Ningxia Daily [宁夏日报] via The Paper [澎湃], 27 November 2018, online. "><sup>&nbsp;[414]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>同年，香港政府的反恐专责组也高调访问新疆。<span id="easy-footnote-415-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-415-672976" title="Christy Leung, ‘Hong Kong’s anti-terrorism task force goes to Xinjiang to study local methods, as China rejects international calls to investigate mass internment centres’, South China Morning Post, 8 December 2018, online."><sup>&nbsp;[415]&nbsp;</sup></a></span></p><p>研究人员应该进一步分析中国大规模政治运动的心理驱动因素、其产生的集体创伤以及社会影响。许多在文化大革命期间经历过个人创伤的高级官员都在近年以高涨的革命热情帮助策划了新疆的镇压。其中最引人瞩目的两个例子是朱海仑和习近平。两人在青少年时期都接受过再教育——朱海仑在新疆，<span id="easy-footnote-416-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-416-672976" title="‘Zhu Hailun: Pioneer of the capital of the western region’ [朱海仑：西域首府引路人], Youth China News [中华儿女新闻网], 19 September 2012, online. "><sup>&nbsp;[416]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>习近平在陕西农村。<span id="easy-footnote-417-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-417-672976" title="Andreas Lorenz, ‘“Redder than red”: An American portrait of China’s next leader’, Spiegel International, 12 May 2010, online; Evan Osnos, ‘Born red: How Xi Jinping, an unremarkable provincial administrator, became China’s most authoritarian leader since Mao’, The New Yorker, 30 March 2015, online. "><sup>&nbsp;[417]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>他们两人后来后声称艰苦劳动的经历磨练、转变了他们的心性。</p><p>在文化大革命期间，习近平的家庭受到迫害。分析人士认为，当年为了度过难关，习近平变得“比红更红”。<span id="easy-footnote-418-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-418-672976" title="Ibid."><sup>&nbsp;[418]&nbsp;</sup></a></span>如今借用毛泽东的手段，他调动了中国官僚系统的大量资源，在全国范围内制造稳定和服从，维吾尔和其他原住民社区首当其冲。本文探讨的两项运动已经导致新疆汉人和原住民社区之间越来越难以互信、彼此怨恨。<span id="easy-footnote-419-672976" class="easy-footnote-margin-adjust"></span><span class="easy-footnote"><a href="#easy-footnote-bottom-419-672976" title="Darren Byler, ‘“Uyghurs are so bad”: Chinese dinner table politics in Xinjiang’, SupChina, 3 June 2020, online."><sup>&nbsp;[419]&nbsp;</sup></a></span></p><p>没有在党国系统内进行的根本的清算，没有在整个中国社会上对种族关系和定居殖民主义更广泛的反思，新疆运动式的政策难以被撤回，两次运动中产生的无数冤案也不会得到平反。</p><div
